Illtay eshay cryay over“Lay, old-hattedgay, igh-bouncinghay overlay,
Iay ustmay avehay ou!yay”

Omasthay Arkepay Invilliersd’ay


Iay

Inay myay oungeryay anday oremay ulnerablevay earsyay myay atherfay avegay emay omesay adviceay
atthay I’veay eenbay urningtay overay inay myay indmay everay incesay.

enever“Whay ouyay eelfay ikelay iticizingcray anyone,ay” ehay oldtay emay, ust“jay
ememberray atthay allay ethay eoplepay inay isthay orldway aven’thay adhay ethay advantagesay
atthay ou’veyay ad.hay”

Ehay idn’tday aysay anyay oremay, utbay e’veway alwaysay eenbay unusuallyay ommunicativecay
inay aay eservedray ayway, anday Iay understooday atthay ehay eantmay aay eatgray ealday oremay
anthay atthay. Inay onsequencecay, I’may inclineday otay eserveray allay udgementsjay, aay
abithay atthay ashay openeday upay anymay uriouscay aturesnay otay emay anday alsoay ademay emay
ethay ictimvay ofay otnay aay ewfay eteranvay oresbay. Ethay abnormalay indmay isay uickqay otay
etectday anday attachay itselfay otay isthay ualityqay enwhay itay appearsay inay aay ormalnay
ersonpay, anday osay itay amecay aboutay atthay inay ollegecay Iay asway unjustlyay accuseday ofay
eingbay aay oliticianpay, ecausebay Iay asway ivypray otay ethay ecretsay iefsgray ofay ildway,
unknownay enmay. Ostmay ofay ethay onfidencescay ereway unsought—frequentlyay Iay avehay
eignedfay eepslay, eoccupationpray, oray aay ostilehay evitylay enwhay Iay ealizedray byay
omesay unmistakableay ignsay atthay anay intimateay evelationray asway uiveringqay onay
ethay orizonhay; orfay ethay intimateay evelationsray ofay oungyay enmay, oray atay eastlay
ethay ermstay inay ichwhay eythay expressay emthay, areay usuallyay agiaristicplay anday
arredmay byay obviousay uppressionssay. Eservingray udgementsjay isay aay attermay ofay
infiniteay opehay. Iay amay illstay aay ittlelay afraiday ofay issingmay omethingsay ifay Iay
orgetfay atthay, asay myay atherfay obbishlysnay uggestedsay, anday Iay obbishlysnay
epeatray, aay ensesay ofay ethay undamentalfay ecenciesday isay arcelledpay outay
unequallyay atay irthbay.

Anday, afteray oastingbay isthay ayway ofay myay olerancetay, Iay omecay otay ethay admissionay
atthay itay ashay aay imitlay. Onductcay aymay ebay oundedfay onay ethay ardhay ockray oray ethay
etway arshesmay, utbay afteray aay ertaincay ointpay Iay on’tday arecay atwhay it’say oundedfay
onay. Enwhay Iay amecay ackbay omfray ethay Eastay astlay autumnay Iay eltfay atthay Iay antedway
ethay orldway otay ebay inay uniformay anday atay aay ortsay ofay oralmay attentionay oreverfay; Iay
antedway onay oremay iotousray excursionsay ithway ivilegedpray impsesglay intoay ethay
umanhay earthay. Onlyay Atsbygay, ethay anmay owhay ivesgay ishay amenay otay isthay ookbay, asway
exemptay omfray myay eaction—Gatsbyray, owhay epresentedray everythingay orfay ichwhay Iay
avehay anay unaffecteday ornscay. Ifay ersonalitypay isay anay unbrokenay eriessay ofay
uccessfulsay esturesgay, enthay erethay asway omethingsay orgeousgay aboutay imhay, omesay
eightenedhay ensitivitysay otay ethay omisespray ofay ifelay, asay ifay ehay ereway elatedray
otay oneay ofay osethay intricateay achinesmay atthay egisterray earthquakesay entay
ousandthay ilesmay awayay. Isthay esponsivenessray adhay othingnay otay oday ithway atthay
abbyflay impressionabilityay ichwhay isay ignifiedday underay ethay amenay ofay ethay
eative“cray emperament”—ittay asway anay extraordinaryay iftgay orfay opehay, aay
omanticray eadinessray uchsay asay Iay avehay evernay oundfay inay anyay otheray ersonpay anday
ichwhay itay isay otnay ikelylay Iay allshay everay indfay againay. O—Gatsbynay urnedtay outay
allay ightray atay ethay enday; itay isay atwhay eyedpray onay Atsbygay, atwhay oulfay ustday
oatedflay inay ethay akeway ofay ishay eamsdray atthay emporarilytay osedclay outay myay
interestay inay ethay abortiveay orrowssay anday ort-windedshay elationsay ofay enmay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Myay amilyfay avehay eenbay ominentpray, ell-to-doway eoplepay inay isthay Iddlemay
Esternway itycay orfay eethray enerationsgay. Ethay Arrawayscay areay omethingsay ofay aay
anclay, anday eway avehay aay aditiontray atthay e’reway escendedday omfray ethay Ukesday ofay
Uccleuchbay, utbay ethay actualay ounderfay ofay myay inelay asway myay andfather’sgray
otherbray, owhay amecay erehay inay ifty-onefay, entsay aay ubstitutesay otay ethay Ivilcay
Arway, anday artedstay ethay olesalewhay ardwarehay usinessbay atthay myay atherfay
arriescay onay odaytay.

Iay evernay awsay isthay eat-unclegray, utbay I’may upposedsay otay ooklay ikelay im—withhay
ecialspay eferenceray otay ethay atherray ard-boiledhay aintingpay atthay angshay inay
ather’sfay officeay. Iay aduatedgray omfray Ewnay Avenhay inay 1915ay, ustjay aay uarterqay ofay
aay enturycay afteray myay atherfay, anday aay ittlelay aterlay Iay articipatedpay inay atthay
elayedday Eutonictay igrationmay ownknay asay ethay Eatgray Arway. Iay enjoyeday ethay
ounter-raidcay osay oroughlythay atthay Iay amecay ackbay estlessray. Insteaday ofay eingbay
ethay armway entrecay ofay ethay orldway, ethay Iddlemay Estway ownay eemedsay ikelay ethay
aggedray edgeay ofay ethay universe—soay Iay ecidedday otay ogay Eastay anday earnlay ethay ondbay
usinessbay. Everybodyay Iay ewknay asway inay ethay ondbay usinessbay, osay Iay upposedsay itay
ouldcay upportsay oneay oremay inglesay anmay. Allay myay auntsay anday unclesay alkedtay itay
overay asay ifay eythay ereway oosingchay aay eppray oolschay orfay emay, anday inallyfay aidsay,
e-es,“Why—yay” ithway eryvay avegray, esitanthay acesfay. Atherfay agreeday otay inancefay
emay orfay aay earyay, anday afteray ariousvay elaysday Iay amecay Eastay, ermanentlypay, Iay
oughtthay, inay ethay ingspray ofay enty-twotway.

Ethay acticalpray ingthay asway otay indfay oomsray inay ethay itycay, utbay itay asway aay armway
easonsay, anday Iay adhay ustjay eftlay aay ountrycay ofay ideway awnslay anday iendlyfray
eestray, osay enwhay aay oungyay anmay atay ethay officeay uggestedsay atthay eway aketay aay
ousehay ogethertay inay aay ommutingcay owntay, itay oundedsay ikelay aay eatgray ideaay. Ehay
oundfay ethay ousehay, aay eather-beatenway ardboardcay ungalowbay atay eightyay aay
onthmay, utbay atay ethay astlay inutemay ethay irmfay ordereday imhay otay Ashingtonway, anday
Iay entway outay otay ethay ountrycay aloneay. Iay adhay aay og—atday eastlay Iay adhay imhay orfay aay
ewfay aysday untilay ehay anray away—anday anay olday Odgeday anday aay Innishfay omanway, owhay
ademay myay edbay anday ookedcay eakfastbray anday utteredmay Innishfay isdomway otay
erselfhay overay ethay electricay ovestay.

Itay asway onelylay orfay aay ayday oray osay untilay oneay orningmay omesay anmay, oremay
ecentlyray arriveday anthay Iay, oppedstay emay onay ethay oadray.

ow“Hay oday ouyay etgay otay Estway Eggay illage?vay” ehay askeday elplesslyhay.

Iay oldtay imhay. Anday asay Iay alkedway onay Iay asway onelylay onay ongerlay. Iay asway aay uidegay,
aay athfinderpay, anay originalay ettlersay. Ehay adhay asuallycay onferredcay onay emay ethay
eedomfray ofay ethay eighbourhoodnay.

Anday osay ithway ethay unshinesay anday ethay eatgray urstsbay ofay eaveslay owinggray onay ethay
eestray, ustjay asay ingsthay owgray inay astfay oviesmay, Iay adhay atthay amiliarfay
onvictioncay atthay ifelay asway eginningbay overay againay ithway ethay ummersay.

Erethay asway osay uchmay otay eadray, orfay oneay ingthay, anday osay uchmay inefay ealthhay otay
ebay ulledpay ownday outay ofay ethay oungyay eath-givingbray airay. Iay oughtbay aay ozenday
olumesvay onay ankingbay anday editcray anday investmentay ecuritiessay, anday eythay
oodstay onay myay elfshay inay edray anday oldgay ikelay ewnay oneymay omfray ethay intmay,
omisingpray otay unfolday ethay iningshay ecretssay atthay onlyay Idasmay anday Organmay anday
Aecenasmay ewknay. Anday Iay adhay ethay ighhay intentionay ofay eadingray anymay otheray
ooksbay esidesbay. Iay asway atherray iterarylay inay ollege—onecay earyay Iay otewray aay
eriessay ofay eryvay olemnsay anday obviousay editorialsay orfay ethay Aleyay Ews—andnay ownay
Iay asway oinggay otay ingbray ackbay allay uchsay ingsthay intoay myay ifelay anday ecomebay
againay atthay ostmay imitedlay ofay allay ecialistsspay, ethay ell-rounded“way an.may”
Isthay isn’tay ustjay anay epigram—lifeay isay uchmay oremay uccessfullysay ookedlay atay
omfray aay inglesay indowway, afteray allay.

Itay asway aay attermay ofay ancechay atthay Iay ouldshay avehay entedray aay ousehay inay oneay ofay
ethay angeststray ommunitiescay inay Orthnay Americaay. Itay asway onay atthay enderslay
iotousray islanday ichwhay extendsay itselfay ueday eastay ofay Ewnay Ork—andyay erewhay
erethay areay, amongay otheray aturalnay uriositiescay, otway unusualay ormationsfay ofay
andlay. Entytway ilesmay omfray ethay itycay aay airpay ofay enormousay eggsay, identicalay inay
ontourcay anday eparatedsay onlyay byay aay ourtesycay aybay, utjay outay intoay ethay ostmay
omesticatedday odybay ofay altsay aterway inay ethay Esternway emispherehay, ethay eatgray
etway arnyardbay ofay Onglay Islanday Oundsay. Eythay areay otnay erfectpay ovals—likeay ethay
eggay inay ethay Olumbuscay orystay, eythay areay othbay ushedcray atflay atay ethay ontactcay
end—butay eirthay icalphysay esemblanceray ustmay ebay aay ourcesay ofay erpetualpay
onderway otay ethay ullsgay atthay flyay overheaday. Otay ethay inglessway aay oremay
interestingay enomenonphay isay eirthay issimilarityday inay everyay articularpay
exceptay apeshay anday izesay.

Iay ivedlay atay Estway Eggay, e—wellthay, ethay esslay ashionablefay ofay ethay otway, oughthay
isthay isay aay ostmay uperficialsay agtay otay expressay ethay izarrebay anday otnay aay ittlelay
inistersay ontrastcay etweenbay emthay. Myay ousehay asway atay ethay eryvay iptay ofay ethay
eggay, onlyay iftyfay ardsyay omfray ethay Oundsay, anday ueezedsqay etweenbay otway ugehay
acesplay atthay entedray orfay elvetway oray ifteenfay ousandthay aay easonsay. Ethay oneay onay
myay ightray asway aay olossalcay affairay byay anyay andard—itstay asway aay actualfay
imitationay ofay omesay Elhôtay eday Illevay inay Ormandynay, ithway aay owertay onay oneay
idesay, ankingspay ewnay underay aay inthay eardbay ofay awray ivyay, anday aay arblemay
immingsway oolpay, anday oremay anthay ortyfay acresay ofay awnlay anday ardengay. Itay asway
Atsby’sgay ansionmay. Oray, atherray, asay Iay idn’tday owknay Mray. Atsbygay, itay asway aay
ansionmay inhabiteday byay aay entlemangay ofay atthay amenay. Myay ownay ousehay asway anay
eyesoreay, utbay itay asway aay allsmay eyesoreay, anday itay adhay eenbay overlookeday, osay Iay
adhay aay iewvay ofay ethay aterway, aay artialpay iewvay ofay myay eighbour’snay awnlay, anday
ethay onsolingcay oximitypray ofay illionaires—allmay orfay eightyay ollarsday aay
onthmay.

Acrossay ethay ourtesycay aybay ethay itewhay alacespay ofay ashionablefay Eastay Eggay
itteredglay alongay ethay aterway, anday ethay istoryhay ofay ethay ummersay eallyray eginsbay
onay ethay eveningay Iay ovedray overay erethay otay avehay innerday ithway ethay Omtay
Uchanansbay. Aisyday asway myay econdsay ousincay onceay emovedray, anday I’day ownknay Omtay
inay ollegecay. Anday ustjay afteray ethay arway Iay entspay otway aysday ithway emthay inay
Icagochay.

Erhay usbandhay, amongay ariousvay icalphysay accomplishmentsay, adhay eenbay oneay ofay
ethay ostmay owerfulpay endsay atthay everay ayedplay ootballfay atay Ewnay Aven—ahay
ationalnay igurefay inay aay ayway, oneay ofay osethay enmay owhay eachray uchsay anay acuteay
imitedlay excellenceay atay enty-onetway atthay everythingay afterwarday avourssay ofay
anticlimaxay. Ishay amilyfay ereway enormouslyay ealthy—evenway inay ollegecay ishay
eedomfray ithway oneymay asway aay attermay orfay eproach—butray ownay e’dhay eftlay Icagochay
anday omecay Eastay inay aay ashionfay atthay atherray ooktay ouryay eathbray awayay: orfay
instanceay, e’dhay oughtbray ownday aay ingstray ofay olopay oniespay omfray Akelay
Orestfay. Itay asway ardhay otay ealizeray atthay aay anmay inay myay ownay enerationgay asway
ealthyway enoughay otay oday atthay.

Whyay eythay amecay Eastay Iay on’tday owknay. Eythay adhay entspay aay earyay inay Ancefray orfay
onay articularpay easonray, anday enthay ifteddray erehay anday erethay unrestfullyay
ereverwhay eoplepay ayedplay olopay anday ereway ichray ogethertay. Isthay asway aay
ermanentpay ovemay, aidsay Aisyday overay ethay elephonetay, utbay Iay idn’tday elievebay
it—Iay adhay onay ightsay intoay Aisy’sday earthay, utbay Iay eltfay atthay Omtay ouldway iftdray
onay oreverfay eekingsay, aay ittlelay istfullyway, orfay ethay amaticdray urbulencetay ofay
omesay irrecoverableay ootballfay amegay.

Anday osay itay appenedhay atthay onay aay armway indyway eveningay Iay ovedray overay otay Eastay
Eggay otay eesay otway olday iendsfray omwhay Iay arcelyscay ewknay atay allay. Eirthay ousehay
asway evenay oremay elaborateay anthay Iay expecteday, aay eerfulchay ed-and-whiteray
Eorgiangay Olonialcay ansionmay, overlookingay ethay aybay. Ethay awnlay artedstay atay
ethay eachbay anday anray owardstay ethay ontfray oorday orfay aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay,
umpingjay overay undialssay anday ickbray alksway anday urningbay ardens—finallygay enwhay
itay eachedray ethay ousehay iftingdray upay ethay idesay inay ightbray inesvay asay oughthay
omfray ethay omentummay ofay itsay unray. Ethay ontfray asway okenbray byay aay inelay ofay Enchfray
indowsway, owingglay ownay ithway eflectedray oldgay anday ideway openay otay ethay armway
indyway afternoonay, anday Omtay Uchananbay inay idingray othesclay asway andingstay ithway
ishay egslay apartay onay ethay ontfray orchpay.

Ehay adhay angedchay incesay ishay Ewnay Avenhay earsyay. Ownay ehay asway aay urdystay
aw-hairedstray anmay ofay irtythay, ithway aay atherray ardhay outhmay anday aay
upercilioussay annermay. Otway iningshay arrogantay eyesay adhay establisheday
ominanceday overay ishay acefay anday avegay imhay ethay appearanceay ofay alwaysay eaninglay
aggressivelyay orwardfay. Otnay evenay ethay effeminateay anksway ofay ishay idingray
othesclay ouldcay idehay ethay enormousay owerpay ofay atthay ody—hebay eemedsay otay illfay
osethay isteningglay ootsbay untilay ehay ainedstray ethay optay acinglay, anday ouyay ouldcay
eesay aay eatgray ackpay ofay usclemay iftingshay enwhay ishay ouldershay ovedmay underay ishay
inthay oatcay. Itay asway aay odybay apablecay ofay enormousay everage—alay uelcray odybay.

Ishay eakingspay oicevay, aay uffgray uskyhay enortay, addeday otay ethay impressionay ofay
actiousnessfray ehay onveyedcay. Erethay asway aay ouchtay ofay aternalpay ontemptcay inay
itay, evenay owardtay eoplepay ehay iked—andlay erethay ereway enmay atay Ewnay Avenhay owhay
adhay atedhay ishay utsgay.

ow“Nay, on’tday inkthay myay opinionay onay esethay attersmay isay inal,fay” ehay eemedsay otay
aysay, ust“jay ecausebay I’may ongerstray anday oremay ofay aay anmay anthay ouyay are.ay” Eway
ereway inay ethay amesay eniorsay ocietysay, anday ilewhay eway ereway evernay intimateay Iay
alwaysay adhay ethay impressionay atthay ehay approveday ofay emay anday antedway emay otay ikelay
imhay ithway omesay arshhay, efiantday istfulnessway ofay ishay ownay.

Eway alkedtay orfay aay ewfay inutesmay onay ethay unnysay orchpay.

I’ve“ay otgay aay icenay aceplay ere,hay” ehay aidsay, ishay eyesay ashingflay aboutay
estlesslyray.

Urningtay emay arounday byay oneay armay, ehay ovedmay aay oadbray atflay andhay alongay ethay
ontfray istavay, includingay inay itsay eepsway aay unkensay Italianay ardengay, aay alfhay
acreay ofay eepday, ungentpay osesray, anday aay ub-nosedsnay otorboatmay atthay umpedbay
ethay idetay offshoreay.

It“ay elongedbay otay Emaineday, ethay oilay an.may” Ehay urnedtay emay arounday againay,
olitelypay anday abruptlyay. e’ll“Way ogay inside.ay”

Eway alkedway oughthray aay ighhay allwayhay intoay aay ightbray osy-colouredray acespay,
agilelyfray oundbay intoay ethay ousehay byay Enchfray indowsway atay eitheray enday. Ethay
indowsway ereway ajaray anday eamingglay itewhay againstay ethay eshfray assgray outsideay
atthay eemedsay otay owgray aay ittlelay ayway intoay ethay ousehay. Aay eezebray ewblay oughthray
ethay oomray, ewblay urtainscay inay atay oneay enday anday outay ethay otheray ikelay alepay
agsflay, istingtway emthay upay owardtay ethay ostedfray edding-cakeway ofay ethay
eilingcay, anday enthay ippledray overay ethay ine-colouredway ugray, akingmay aay adowshay
onay itay asay indway oesday onay ethay easay.

Ethay onlyay ompletelycay ationarystay objectay inay ethay oomray asway anay enormousay
ouchcay onay ichwhay otway oungyay omenway ereway uoyedbay upay asay oughthay uponay anay
anchoreday alloonbay. Eythay ereway othbay inay itewhay, anday eirthay essesdray ereway
ipplingray anday utteringflay asay ifay eythay adhay ustjay eenbay ownblay ackbay inay afteray aay
ortshay ightflay arounday ethay ousehay. Iay ustmay avehay oodstay orfay aay ewfay omentsmay
isteninglay otay ethay ipwhay anday apsnay ofay ethay urtainscay anday ethay oangray ofay aay
icturepay onay ethay allway. Enthay erethay asway aay oombay asay Omtay Uchananbay utshay ethay
earray indowsway anday ethay aughtcay indway iedday outay aboutay ethay oomray, anday ethay
urtainscay anday ethay ugsray anday ethay otway oungyay omenway alloonedbay owlyslay otay ethay
oorflay.

Ethay oungeryay ofay ethay otway asway aay angerstray otay emay. Eshay asway extendeday ullfay
engthlay atay erhay enday ofay ethay ivanday, ompletelycay otionlessmay, anday ithway erhay
inchay aisedray aay ittlelay, asay ifay eshay ereway alancingbay omethingsay onay itay ichwhay
asway uiteqay ikelylay otay allfay. Ifay eshay awsay emay outay ofay ethay ornercay ofay erhay eyesay
eshay avegay onay inthay ofay it—indeeday, Iay asway almostay urprisedsay intoay urmuringmay
anay apologyay orfay avinghay isturbedday erhay byay omingcay inay.

Ethay otheray irlgay, Aisyday, ademay anay attemptay otay ise—sheray eanedlay ightlyslay
orwardfay ithway aay onscientiouscay expression—thenay eshay aughedlay, anay absurday,
armingchay ittlelay aughlay, anday Iay aughedlay ootay anday amecay orwardfay intoay ethay
oomray.

I’m“ay aralysedp-pay ithway appiness.hay”

Eshay aughedlay againay, asay ifay eshay aidsay omethingsay eryvay ittyway, anday eldhay myay
andhay orfay aay omentmay, ookinglay upay intoay myay acefay, omisingpray atthay erethay asway
onay oneay inay ethay orldway eshay osay uchmay antedway otay eesay. Atthay asway aay ayway eshay
adhay. Eshay intedhay inay aay urmurmay atthay ethay urnamesay ofay ethay alancingbay irlgay asway
Akerbay. I’ve(ay eardhay itay aidsay atthay Aisy’sday urmurmay asway onlyay otay akemay eoplepay
eanlay owardtay erhay; anay irrelevantay iticismcray atthay ademay itay onay esslay
arming.chay)

Atay anyay ateray, Issmay Aker’sbay ipslay utteredflay, eshay oddednay atay emay almostay
imperceptiblyay, anday enthay uicklyqay ippedtay erhay eadhay ackbay again—theay objectay

Ofay oursecay Iay ewknay atwhay eythay ereway eferringray otay, utbay Iay asn’tway evenay

Eirthay interestay atherray ouchedtay emay anday ademay emthay esslay emotelyray

alestay ideasay asay ifay ishay urdystay icalphysay egotismay onay ongerlay ourishednay ishay
eremptorypay earthay.

Alreadyay itay asway eepday ummersay onay oadhouseray oofsray anday inay ontfray ofay aysideway
aragesgay, erewhay ewnay edray etrol-pumpspay atsay outay inay oolspay ofay ightlay, anday

ewblay ethay ogsfray ullfay ofay ifelay. Ethay ilhouettesay ofay aay ovingmay atcay averedway
acrossay ethay oonlightmay, anday, urningtay myay eadhay otay atchway itay, Iay awsay atthay Iay
asway otnay alone—fiftyay eetfay awayay aay igurefay adhay emergeday omfray ethay adowshay ofay
myay eighbour’snay ansionmay anday asway andingstay ithway ishay andshay inay ishay ocketspay
egardingray ethay ilversay epperpay ofay ethay arsstay. Omethingsay inay ishay eisurelylay
ovementsmay anday ethay ecuresay ositionpay ofay ishay eetfay uponay ethay awnlay uggestedsay
atthay itay asway Mray. Atsbygay imselfhay, omecay outay otay etermineday atwhay areshay asway
ishay ofay ouray ocallay eavenshay.

Iay ecidedday otay allcay otay imhay. Issmay Akerbay adhay entionedmay imhay atay innerday, anday
atthay ouldway oday orfay anay introductionay. Utbay Iay idn’tday allcay otay imhay, orfay ehay
avegay aay uddensay intimationay atthay ehay asway ontentcay otay ebay alone—heay etchedstray
outay ishay armsay owardtay ethay arkday aterway inay aay uriouscay ayway, anday, arfay asay Iay asway
omfray imhay, Iay ouldcay avehay ornsway ehay asway emblingtray. Involuntarilyay Iay ancedglay
eaward—andsay istinguishedday othingnay exceptay aay inglesay eengray ightlay, inutemay
anday arfay awayay, atthay ightmay avehay eenbay ethay enday ofay aay ockday. Enwhay Iay ookedlay
onceay oremay orfay Atsbygay ehay adhay anishedvay, anday Iay asway aloneay againay inay ethay
unquietay arknessday.


IIay

Aboutay alfwayhay etweenbay Estway Eggay anday Ewnay Orkyay ethay otormay oadray astilyhay
oinsjay ethay ailroadray anday unsray esidebay itay orfay aay uarterqay ofay aay ilemay, osay asay
otay inkshray awayay omfray aay ertaincay esolateday areaay ofay andlay. Isthay isay aay alleyvay
ofay ashes—aay antasticfay armfay erewhay ashesay owgray ikelay eatwhay intoay idgesray anday
illshay anday otesquegray ardensgay; erewhay ashesay aketay ethay ormsfay ofay ouseshay anday
imneyschay anday isingray okesmay anday, inallyfay, ithway aay anscendenttray effortay, ofay
ash-greyay enmay, owhay ovemay imlyday anday alreadyay umblingcray oughthray ethay owderypay
airay. Occasionallyay aay inelay ofay eygray arscay awlscray alongay anay invisibleay acktray,
ivesgay outay aay astlyghay eakcray, anday omescay otay estray, anday immediatelyay ethay
ash-greyay enmay armsway upay ithway eadenlay adesspay anday irstay upay anay impenetrableay
oudclay, ichwhay eensscray eirthay obscureay operationsay omfray ouryay ightsay.

Utbay aboveay ethay eygray andlay anday ethay asmsspay ofay eakblay ustday ichwhay iftdray
endlesslyay overay itay, ouyay erceivepay, afteray aay omentmay, ethay eyesay ofay Octorday Tay.
Jay. Eckleburgay. Ethay eyesay ofay Octorday Tay. Jay. Eckleburgay areay ueblay anday
igantic—theirgay etinasray areay oneay ardyay ighhay. Eythay ooklay outay ofay onay acefay,
utbay, insteaday, omfray aay airpay ofay enormousay ellowyay ectaclesspay ichwhay asspay
overay aay onexistentnay osenay. Evidentlyay omesay ildway agway ofay anay oculistay etsay
emthay erethay otay attenfay ishay acticepray inay ethay oroughbay ofay Ueensqay, anday enthay
anksay ownday imselfhay intoay eternalay indnessblay, oray orgotfay emthay anday ovedmay
awayay. Utbay ishay eyesay, immedday aay ittlelay byay anymay aintlesspay aysday, underay unsay
anday ainray, oodbray onay overay ethay olemnsay umpingday oundgray.

Ethay alleyvay ofay ashesay isay oundedbay onay oneay idesay byay aay allsmay oulfay iverray, anday,
enwhay ethay awbridgedray isay upay otay etlay argesbay oughthray, ethay assengerspay onay
aitingway ainstray ancay arestay atay ethay ismalday enescay orfay asay onglay asay alfhay anay
ourhay. Erethay isay alwaysay aay althay erethay ofay atay eastlay aay inutemay, anday itay asway
ecausebay ofay isthay atthay Iay irstfay etmay Omtay Uchanan’sbay istressmay.

Ethay actfay atthay ehay adhay oneay asway insisteday uponay ereverwhay ehay asway ownknay. Ishay
acquaintancesay esentedray ethay actfay atthay ehay urnedtay upay inay opularpay aféscay
ithway erhay anday, eavinglay erhay atay aay abletay, aunteredsay aboutay, attingchay ithway
omsoeverwhay ehay ewknay. Oughthay Iay asway uriouscay otay eesay erhay, Iay adhay onay esireday
otay eetmay er—buthay Iay idday. Iay entway upay otay Ewnay Orkyay ithway Omtay onay ethay aintray oneay
afternoonay, anday enwhay eway oppedstay byay ethay ash-heapsay ehay umpedjay otay ishay eetfay
anday, akingtay oldhay ofay myay elboway, iterallylay orcedfay emay omfray ethay arcay.

e’re“Way ettinggay off,ay” ehay insisteday. I“ay antway ouyay otay eetmay myay irl.gay”

Iay inkthay e’dhay ankedtay upay aay oodgay ealday atay uncheonlay, anday ishay eterminationday
otay avehay myay ompanycay orderedbay onay iolencevay. Ethay upercilioussay assumptionay
asway atthay onay Undaysay afternoonay Iay adhay othingnay etterbay otay oday.

Iay ollowedfay imhay overay aay owlay itewashedwhay ailroadray encefay, anday eway alkedway
ackbay aay undredhay ardsyay alongay ethay oadray underay Octorday Eckleburg’say
ersistentpay arestay. Ethay onlyay uildingbay inay ightsay asway aay allsmay ockblay ofay
ellowyay ickbray ittingsay onay ethay edgeay ofay ethay asteway andlay, aay ortsay ofay ompactcay
Ainmay Eetstray inisteringmay otay itay, anday ontiguouscay otay absolutelyay othingnay.
Oneay ofay ethay eethray opsshay itay ontainedcay asway orfay entray anday anotheray asway anay
all-nightay estaurantray, approacheday byay aay ailtray ofay ashesay; ethay irdthay asway aay
arage—Repairsgay. Eorgegay Bay. Ilsonway. Arscay oughtbay anday old.—andsay Iay ollowedfay
Omtay insideay.

Ethay interioray asway unprosperousay anday arebay; ethay onlyay arcay isiblevay asway ethay

umptuoussay anday omanticray apartmentsay ereway oncealedcay overheaday, enwhay ethay

aintlyfay andsomehay. Enwhay ehay awsay usay aay ampday eamglay ofay opehay angspray intoay ishay

Atay 158thay Eetstray ethay abcay oppedstay atay oneay iceslay inay aay onglay itewhay akecay ofay

I’m“ay oinggay otay avehay ethay EesmcKay omecay up,ay” eshay announceday asay eway oseray inay
ethay elevatoray. And“ay, ofay oursecay, Iay otgay otay allcay upay myay istersay, oo.tay”

Ethay apartmentay asway onay ethay optay oor—aflay allsmay iving-roomlay, aay allsmay
ining-roomday, aay allsmay edroombay, anday aay athbay. Ethay iving-roomlay asway owdedcray
otay ethay oorsday ithway aay etsay ofay apestriedtay urniturefay entirelyay ootay argelay orfay
itay, osay atthay otay ovemay aboutay asway otay umblestay ontinuallycay overay enesscay ofay
adieslay ingingsway inay ethay ardensgay ofay Ersaillesvay. Ethay onlyay icturepay asway anay
over-enlargeday otographphay, apparentlyay aay enhay ittingsay onay aay urredblay ockray.
Ookedlay atay omfray aay istanceday, oweverhay, ethay enhay esolvedray itselfay intoay aay
onnetbay, anday ethay ountenancecay ofay aay outstay olday adylay eamedbay ownday intoay ethay
oomray. Everalsay olday opiescay ofay Owntay Attletay aylay onay ethay abletay ogethertay ithway
aay opycay ofay Imonsay Alledcay Eterpay, anday omesay ofay ethay allsmay andalscay agazinesmay
ofay Oadwaybray. Mrsay. Ilsonway asway irstfay oncernedcay ithway ethay ogday. Aay eluctantray
elevatoray oybay entway orfay aay oxbay ullfay ofay awstray anday omesay ilkmay, otay ichwhay ehay
addeday onay ishay ownay initiativeay aay intay ofay argelay, ardhay ogday iscuits—onebay ofay
ichwhay ecomposedday apatheticallyay inay ethay aucersay ofay ilkmay allay
afternoonay. Eanwhilemay Omtay oughtbray outay aay ottlebay ofay iskywhay omfray aay ockedlay
ureaubay oorday.

Iay avehay eenbay unkdray ustjay icetway inay myay ifelay, anday ethay econdsay imetay asway atthay
afternoonay; osay everythingay atthay appenedhay ashay aay imday, azyhay astcay overay itay,
althoughay untilay afteray eightay o’clockay ethay apartmentay asway ullfay ofay eerfulchay
unsay. Ittingsay onay Om’stay aplay Mrsay. Ilsonway alledcay upay everalsay eoplepay onay ethay
elephonetay; enthay erethay ereway onay igarettescay, anday Iay entway outay otay uybay omesay
atay ethay ugstoredray onay ethay ornercay. Enwhay Iay amecay ackbay eythay adhay othbay
isappearedday, osay Iay atsay ownday iscreetlyday inay ethay iving-roomlay anday eadray aay
apterchay ofay Imonsay Alledcay Eter—eitherpay itay asway erribletay uffstay oray ethay
iskywhay istortedday ingsthay, ecausebay itay idn’tday akemay anyay ensesay otay emay.

Ustjay asay Omtay anday Emyrtlay after(ay ethay irstfay inkdray Mrsay. Ilsonway anday Iay alledcay
eachay otheray byay ouray irstfay amesnay) eappearedray, ompanycay ommencedcay otay arriveay
atay ethay apartmentay oorday.

Ethay istersay, Atherinecay, asway aay enderslay, orldlyway irlgay ofay aboutay irtythay,
ithway aay olidsay, ickystay obbay ofay edray airhay, anday aay omplexioncay owderedpay ilkymay
itewhay. Erhay eyebrowsay adhay eenbay uckedplay anday enthay awndray onay againay atay aay oremay
akishray angleay, utbay ethay effortsay ofay aturenay owardtay ethay estorationray ofay ethay
olday alignmentay avegay aay urredblay airay otay erhay acefay. Enwhay eshay ovedmay aboutay
erethay asway anay incessantay ickingclay asay innumerableay otterypay aceletsbray
ingledjay upay anday ownday uponay erhay armsay. Eshay amecay inay ithway uchsay aay oprietarypray
astehay, anday ookedlay arounday osay ossessivelypay atay ethay urniturefay atthay Iay
onderedway ifay eshay ivedlay erehay. Utbay enwhay Iay askeday erhay eshay aughedlay
immoderatelyay, epeatedray myay uestionqay alouday, anday oldtay emay eshay ivedlay ithway aay
irlgay iendfray atay aay otelhay.

Mray. EemcKay asway aay alepay, emininefay anmay omfray ethay atflay elowbay. Ehay adhay ustjay
avedshay, orfay erethay asway aay itewhay otspay ofay atherlay onay ishay eekbonechay, anday ehay
asway ostmay espectfulray inay ishay eetinggray otay everyoneay inay ethay oomray. Ehay
informeday emay atthay ehay asway inay ethay artistic“ay ame,gay” anday Iay atheredgay aterlay
atthay ehay asway aay otographerphay anday adhay ademay ethay imday enlargementay ofay
Mrsay. Ilson’sway othermay ichwhay overedhay ikelay anay ectoplasmay onay ethay allway. Ishay
ifeway asway illshray, anguidlay, andsomehay, anday orriblehay. Eshay oldtay emay ithway
idepray atthay erhay usbandhay adhay otographedphay erhay aay undredhay anday enty-seventway
imestay incesay eythay adhay eenbay arriedmay.

Mrsay. Ilsonway adhay angedchay erhay ostumecay omesay imetay eforebay, anday asway ownay
attireday inay anay elaborateay afternoonay essdray ofay eam-colouredcray iffonchay,
ichwhay avegay outay aay ontinualcay ustleray asay eshay eptsway aboutay ethay oomray. Ithway
ethay influenceay ofay ethay essdray erhay ersonalitypay adhay alsoay undergoneay aay
angechay. Ethay intenseay italityvay atthay adhay eenbay osay emarkableray inay ethay aragegay
asway onvertedcay intoay impressiveay auteurhay. Erhay aughterlay, erhay esturesgay, erhay
assertionsay ecamebay oremay iolentlyvay affecteday omentmay byay omentmay, anday asay eshay
expandeday ethay oomray ewgray allersmay arounday erhay, untilay eshay eemedsay otay ebay
evolvingray onay aay oisynay, eakingcray ivotpay oughthray ethay okysmay airay.

IIIay

Erethay asway usicmay omfray myay eighbour’snay ousehay oughthray ethay ummersay ightsnay.
Inay ishay ueblay ardensgay enmay anday irlsgay amecay anday entway ikelay othsmay amongay ethay
isperingswhay anday ethay ampagnechay anday ethay arsstay. Atay ighhay idetay inay ethay
afternoonay Iay atchedway ishay uestsgay ivingday omfray ethay owertay ofay ishay aftray, oray
akingtay ethay unsay onay ethay othay andsay ofay ishay eachbay ilewhay ishay otway otorboatsmay
itslay ethay atersway ofay ethay Oundsay, awingdray aquaplanesay overay ataractscay ofay
oamfay. Onay eekendsway ishay Olls-Royceray ecamebay anay omnibusay, earingbay artiespay
otay anday omfray ethay itycay etweenbay inenay inay ethay orningmay anday onglay astpay
idnightmay, ilewhay ishay ationstay agonway amperedscay ikelay aay iskbray ellowyay ugbay otay
eetmay allay ainstray. Anday onay Ondaysmay eightay ervantssay, includingay anay extraay
ardenergay, oiledtay allay ayday ithway opsmay anday ubbing-brushesscray anday ammershay
anday arden-shearsgay, epairingray ethay avagesray ofay ethay ightnay eforebay.

Everyay Idayfray ivefay atescray ofay orangesay anday emonslay arriveday omfray aay
uitererfray inay Ewnay Ork—everyyay Ondaymay esethay amesay orangesay anday emonslay eftlay
ishay ackbay oorday inay aay amidpyray ofay ulplesspay alveshay. Erethay asway aay achinemay inay
ethay itchenkay ichwhay ouldcay extractay ethay uicejay ofay otway undredhay orangesay inay
alfhay anay ourhay ifay aay ittlelay uttonbay asway essedpray otway undredhay imestay byay aay
utler’sbay umbthay.

Atay eastlay onceay aay ortnightfay aay orpscay ofay atererscay amecay ownday ithway everalsay

Eadingray overay atwhay Iay avehay ittenwray osay arfay, Iay eesay Iay avehay ivengay ethay
impressionay atthay ethay eventsay ofay eethray ightsnay everalsay eeksway apartay ereway

infinitelyay esslay anthay myay ersonalpay affairsay.

Ostmay ofay ethay imetay Iay orkedway. Inay ethay earlyay orningmay ethay unsay ewthray myay
adowshay estwardway asay Iay urriedhay ownday ethay itewhay asmschay ofay owerlay Ewnay Orkyay
otay ethay Obitypray Usttray. Iay ewknay ethay otheray erksclay anday oungyay ond-salesmenbay

estaurantsray onay ittlelay igpay ausagessay anday ashedmay otatoespay anday offeecay. Iay
evenay adhay aay ortshay affairay ithway aay irlgay owhay ivedlay inay Erseyjay Itycay anday
orkedway inay ethay accountingay epartmentday, utbay erhay otherbray eganbay owingthray
eanmay ookslay inay myay irectionday, osay enwhay eshay entway onay erhay acationvay inay Ulyjay Iay
etlay itay owblay uietlyqay awayay.

Iay ooktay innerday usuallyay atay ethay Aleyay Ub—forclay omesay easonray itay asway ethay
oomiestglay eventay ofay myay ay—andday enthay Iay entway upstairsay otay ethay ibrarylay anday
udiedstay investmentsay anday ecuritiessay orfay aay onscientiouscay ourhay. Erethay
ereway enerallygay aay ewfay iotersray arounday, utbay eythay evernay amecay intoay ethay

ellowmay, Iay olledstray ownday Adisonmay Avenueay astpay ethay olday Urraymay Illhay Otelhay,
anday overay 33rday Eetstray otay ethay Ennsylvaniapay Ationstay.

Iay eganbay otay ikelay Ewnay Orkyay, ethay acyray, adventurousay eelfay ofay itay atay ightnay,
anday ethay atisfactionsay atthay ethay onstantcay ickerflay ofay enmay anday omenway anday

owknay oray isapproveday. Ometimessay, inay myay indmay, Iay ollowedfay emthay otay eirthay

iledsmay ackbay atay emay eforebay eythay adedfay oughthray aay oorday intoay armway
arknessday. Atay ethay enchanteday etropolitanmay ilighttway Iay eltfay aay auntinghay
onelinesslay ometimessay, anday eltfay itay inay others—pooray oungyay erksclay owhay

estaurantray inner—youngday erksclay inay ethay uskday, astingway ethay ostmay oignantpay
omentsmay ofay ightnay anday ifelay.

Againay atay eightay o’clockay, enwhay ethay arkday aneslay ofay ethay Ortiesfay ereway inedlay

atthay Iay, ootay, asway urryinghay owardstay aietygay anday aringshay eirthay intimateay

Orfay aay ilewhay Iay ostlay ightsay ofay Ordanjay Akerbay, anday enthay inay idsummermay Iay
oundfay erhay againay. Atay irstfay Iay asway atteredflay otay ogay acesplay ithway erhay,

asway omethingsay oremay. Iay asn’tway actuallyay inay ovelay, utbay Iay eltfay aay ortsay ofay
endertay uriositycay. Ethay oredbay aughtyhay acefay atthay eshay urnedtay otay ethay orldway
oncealedcay omething—mostsay affectationsay oncealcay omethingsay eventuallyay,
evenay oughthay eythay on’tday inay ethay eginning—andbay oneay ayday Iay oundfay atwhay itay

Ordanjay Akerbay instinctivelyay avoideday everclay, ewdshray enmay, anday ownay Iay awsay
atthay isthay asway ecausebay eshay eltfay afersay onay aay aneplay erewhay anyay ivergenceday
omfray aay odecay ouldway ebay oughtthay impossibleay. Eshay asway incurablyay ishonestday.

unwillingnessay, Iay upposesay eshay adhay egunbay ealingday inay ubterfugessay enwhay eshay
asway eryvay oungyay inay orderay otay eepkay atthay oolcay, insolentay ilesmay urnedtay otay
ethay orldway anday etyay atisfysay ethay emandsday ofay erhay ardhay, auntyjay odybay.

Itay ademay onay ifferenceday otay emay. Ishonestyday inay aay omanway isay aay ingthay ouyay
evernay ameblay eeply—Iday asway asuallycay orrysay, anday enthay Iay orgotfay. Itay asway onay
atthay amesay ouse-partyhay atthay eway adhay aay uriouscay onversationcay aboutay ivingdray
aay arcay. Itay artedstay ecausebay eshay assedpay osay oseclay otay omesay orkmenway atthay ouray
enderfay ickedflay aay uttonbay onay oneay an’smay oatcay.

ou’re“Yay aay ottenray iver,dray” Iay otestedpray. Either“ay ouyay oughtay otay ebay oremay
arefulcay, oray ouyay oughtn’tay otay ivedray atay all.ay”

I“ay amay areful.cay”

o“Nay, ou’reyay ot.nay”

ell“Way, otheray eoplepay are,ay” eshay aidsay ightlylay.

at’s“Whay atthay otgay otay oday ithway it?ay”

ey’ll“Thay eepkay outay ofay myay ay,way” eshay insisteday. It“ay akestay otway otay akemay anay
accident.ay”

uppose“Say ouyay etmay omebodysay ustjay asay arelesscay asay ourself.yay”

I“ay opehay Iay evernay ill,way” eshay answereday. I“ay atehay arelesscay eoplepay. At’sthay
whyay Iay ikelay ou.yay”

Erhay eygray, un-strainedsay eyesay aredstay aightstray aheaday, utbay eshay adhay
eliberatelyday iftedshay ouray elationsray, anday orfay aay omentmay Iay oughtthay Iay ovedlay
erhay. Utbay Iay amay ow-thinkingslay anday ullfay ofay interioray ulesray atthay actay asay
akesbray onay myay esiresday, anday Iay ewknay atthay irstfay Iay adhay otay etgay elfmysay
efinitelyday outay ofay atthay angletay ackbay omehay. I’day eenbay itingwray etterslay onceay
aay eekway anday igningsay emthay: ove“Lay, Ick,nay” anday allay Iay ouldcay inkthay ofay asway
owhay, enwhay atthay ertaincay irlgay ayedplay ennistay, aay aintfay oustachemay ofay
erspirationpay appeareday onay erhay upperay iplay. Everthelessnay erethay asway aay aguevay
understandingay atthay adhay otay ebay actfullytay okenbray offay eforebay Iay asway eefray.

Everyoneay uspectssay imselfhay ofay atay eastlay oneay ofay ethay ardinalcay irtuesvay, anday
isthay isay inemay: Iay amay oneay ofay ethay ewfay onesthay eoplepay atthay Iay avehay everay
ownknay.


IVay

Onay Undaysay orningmay ilewhay urchchay ellsbay angray inay ethay illagesvay alongshoreay,
ethay orldway anday itsay istressmay eturnedray otay Atsby’sgay ousehay anday inkledtway
ilariouslyhay onay ishay awnlay.

e’s“Hay aay ootlegger,bay” aidsay ethay oungyay adieslay, ovingmay omewheresay etweenbay
ishay ocktailscay anday ishay owersflay. One“ay imetay ehay illedkay aay anmay owhay adhay oundfay
outay atthay ehay asway ephewnay otay Onvay Indenburghay anday econdsay ousincay otay ethay
evilday. Eachray emay aay oseray, oneyhay, anday ourpay emay aay astlay opdray intoay atthay erethay
alcrystay ass.glay”

Onceay Iay otewray ownday onay ethay emptyay acesspay ofay aay imetabletay ethay amesnay ofay
osethay owhay amecay otay Atsby’sgay ousehay atthay ummersay. Itay isay anay olday imetabletay
ownay, isintegratingday atay itsay oldsfay, anday eadedhay is“Thay eduleschay inay effectay
Ulyjay 5thay, 1922.ay” Utbay Iay ancay illstay eadray ethay eygray amesnay, anday eythay illway
ivegay ouyay aay etterbay impressionay anthay myay eneralitiesgay ofay osethay owhay
accepteday Atsby’sgay ospitalityhay anday aidpay imhay ethay ubtlesay ibutetray ofay
owingknay othingnay ateverwhay aboutay imhay.

Omfray Eastay Eggay, enthay, amecay ethay Esterchay Eckersbay anday ethay Eecheslay, anday aay
anmay amednay Unsenbay, omwhay Iay ewknay atay Aleyay, anday Octorday Ebsterway Ivetcay, owhay
asway owneddray astlay ummersay upay inay Ainemay. Anday ethay Ornbeamshay anday ethay Illieway
Oltairesvay, anday aay olewhay anclay amednay Ackbuckblay, owhay alwaysay atheredgay inay aay
ornercay anday ippedflay upay eirthay osesnay ikelay oatsgay atay osoeverwhay amecay
earnay. Anday ethay Ismaysay anday ethay Ieschrystay or(ay atherray Uberthay Auerbachay anday
Mray. Ie’schrystay ife)way, anday Edgaray Eaverbay, osewhay airhay, eythay aysay, urnedtay
otton-whitecay oneay interway afternoonay orfay onay oodgay easonray atay allay.

Arenceclay Endiveay asway omfray Eastay Eggay, asay Iay ememberray. Ehay amecay onlyay onceay,
inay itewhay ickerbockersknay, anday adhay aay ightfay ithway aay umbay amednay Ettyay inay ethay
ardengay. Omfray artherfay outay onay ethay Islanday amecay ethay Eadleschay anday ethay Oay.
Ray. Pay. Aedersschray, anday ethay Onewallstay Acksonjay Abramsay ofay Eorgiagay, anday ethay
Ishguardsfay anday ethay Ipleyray Ellssnay. Ellsnay asway erethay eethray aysday eforebay ehay
entway otay ethay enitentiarypay, osay unkdray outay onay ethay avelgray ivedray atthay
Mrsay. Ulyssesay Ett’ssway automobileay anray overay ishay ightray andhay. Ethay Anciesday
amecay, ootay, anday Say. Bay. Itebaitwhay, owhay asway ellway overay ixtysay, anday Auricemay
Aay. Inkflay, anday ethay Ammerheadshay, anday Elugabay ethay obaccotay importeray, anday
Eluga’sbay irlsgay.

Omfray Estway Eggay amecay ethay Olespay anday ethay Ulreadysmay anday Ecilcay Oebuckray anday
Ecilcay Oenschay anday Ulickgay ethay Atestay enatorsay anday Ewtonnay Orchiday, owhay
ontrolledcay Ilmsfay Arpay Excellenceay, anday Eckhaustay anday Eclyday Ohencay anday Onday
Say. Artzschway e(thay onsay) anday Arthuray ArtymcCay, allay onnectedcay ithway ethay
oviesmay inay oneay ayway oray anotheray. Anday ethay Atlipscay anday ethay Embergsbay anday Gay.
Earlay Uldoonmay, otherbray otay atthay Uldoonmay owhay afterwarday angledstray ishay
ifeway. Aday Ontanofay ethay omoterpray amecay erethay, anday Eday Egroslay anday Amesjay Bay.
ot-Gut”(“Ray) Erretfay anday ethay Eday Ongsjay anday Ernestay Illy—theylay amecay otay
amblegay, anday enwhay Erretfay anderedway intoay ethay ardengay itay eantmay ehay asway
eanedclay outay anday Associateday Actiontray ouldway avehay otay uctuateflay ofitablypray
extnay ayday.

Aay anmay amednay Ipspringerklay asway erethay osay oftenay atthay ehay ecamebay ownknay asay
e“thay oarder”—Ibay oubtday ifay ehay adhay anyay otheray omehay. Ofay eatricalthay eoplepay
erethay ereway Usgay Aizeway anday Oracehay O’Donavanay anday Esterlay Ermyay anday Eorgegay
Uckweedday anday Ancisfray Ullbay. Alsoay omfray Ewnay Orkyay ereway ethay Omeschray anday ethay
Ackhyssonsbay anday ethay Ennickersday anday Usselray Ettybay anday ethay Orriganscay anday
ethay Elleherskay anday ethay Ewarsday anday ethay Ullysscay anday Say. Way. Elcherbay anday ethay
Irkessmay anday ethay oungyay Uinnsqay, ivorcedday ownay, anday Enryhay Lay. Almettopay, owhay
illedkay imselfhay byay umpingjay inay ontfray ofay aay ubwaysay aintray inay Imestay Uaresqay.

Ennybay EnahanmcClay arriveday alwaysay ithway ourfay irlsgay. Eythay ereway evernay uiteqay
ethay amesay onesay inay icalphysay ersonpay, utbay eythay ereway osay identicalay oneay ithway
anotheray atthay itay inevitablyay eemedsay eythay adhay eenbay erethay eforebay. Iay avehay
orgottenfay eirthay ames—Jaquelinenay, Iay inkthay, oray elseay Onsuelacay, oray Oriaglay
oray Udyjay oray Unejay, anday eirthay astlay amesnay ereway eitheray ethay elodiousmay amesnay
ofay owersflay anday onthsmay oray ethay ernerstay onesay ofay ethay eatgray Americanay
apitalistscay osewhay ousinscay, ifay essedpray, eythay ouldway onfesscay emselvesthay
otay ebay.

Inay additionay otay allay esethay Iay ancay ememberray atthay Austinafay O’Brienay amecay
erethay atay eastlay onceay anday ethay Aedekerbay irlsgay anday oungyay Ewerbray, owhay adhay
ishay osenay otshay offay inay ethay arway, anday Mray. Albrucksburgeray anday Issmay Aaghay,
ishay iancéefay, anday Arditaay Itz-Petersfay anday Mray. Pay. Ewettjay, onceay eadhay ofay
ethay Americanay Egionlay, anday Issmay Audiaclay Iphay, ithway aay anmay eputedray otay ebay
erhay auffeurchay, anday aay incepray ofay omethingsay, omwhay eway alledcay Ukeday, anday
osewhay amenay, ifay Iay everay ewknay itay, Iay avehay orgottenfay.

Allay esethay eoplepay amecay otay Atsby’sgay ousehay inay ethay ummersay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Atay inenay o’clockay, oneay orningmay atelay inay Ulyjay, Atsby’sgay orgeousgay arcay
urchedlay upay ethay ockyray ivedray otay myay oorday anday avegay outay aay urstbay ofay elodymay
omfray itsay ee-notedthray ornhay.

Itay asway ethay irstfay imetay ehay adhay alledcay onay emay, oughthay Iay adhay onegay otay otway ofay
ishay artiespay, ountedmay inay ishay oplanehydray, anday, atay ishay urgentay invitationay,
ademay equentfray useay ofay ishay eachbay.

ood“Gay orningmay, olday ortspay. Ou’reyay avinghay unchlay ithway emay odaytay anday Iay
oughtthay e’dway ideray upay ogether.tay”

Ehay asway alancingbay imselfhay onay ethay ashboardday ofay ishay arcay ithway atthay
esourcefulnessray ofay ovementmay atthay isay osay eculiarlypay American—thatay omescay,
Iay upposesay, ithway ethay absenceay ofay iftinglay orkway inay outhyay anday, evenay oremay,
ithway ethay ormlessfay acegray ofay ouray ervousnay, oradicspay amesgay. Isthay ualityqay
asway ontinuallycay eakingbray oughthray ishay unctiliouspay annermay inay ethay apeshay
ofay estlessnessray. Ehay asway evernay uiteqay illstay; erethay asway alwaysay aay appingtay
ootfay omewheresay oray ethay impatientay openingay anday osingclay ofay aay andhay.

Ehay awsay emay ookinglay ithway admirationay atay ishay arcay.

It’s“ay ettypray, isn’tay itay, olday ort?spay” Ehay umpedjay offay otay ivegay emay aay etterbay
iewvay. aven’t“Hay ouyay everay eensay itay efore?bay”

I’day eensay itay. Everybodyay adhay eensay itay. Itay asway aay ichray eamcray olourcay, ightbray
ithway ickelnay, ollensway erehay anday erethay inay itsay onstrousmay engthlay ithway
iumphanttray atboxeshay anday upper-boxessay anday oolboxestay, anday erracedtay ithway
aay abyrinthlay ofay indshieldsway atthay irroredmay aay ozenday unssay. Ittingsay ownday
ehindbay anymay ayerslay ofay assglay inay aay ortsay ofay eengray eatherlay onservatorycay,
eway artedstay otay owntay.

Iay adhay alkedtay ithway imhay erhapspay alfhay aay ozenday imestay inay ethay astpay onthmay anday
oundfay, otay myay isappointmentday, atthay ehay adhay ittlelay otay aysay. Osay myay irstfay
impressionay, atthay ehay asway aay ersonpay ofay omesay undefineday onsequencecay, adhay
aduallygray adedfay anday ehay adhay ecomebay implysay ethay oprietorpray ofay anay
elaborateay oadhouseray extnay oorday.

Anday enthay amecay atthay isconcertingday ideray. Eway adn’thay eachedray Estway Eggay
illagevay eforebay Atsbygay eganbay eavinglay ishay elegantay entencessay unfinisheday
anday appingslay imselfhay indecisivelyay onay ethay eeknay ofay ishay aramel-colouredcay
uitsay.

ook“Lay erehay, olday ort,spay” ehay okebray outay urprisinglysay, at’s“whay ouryay
opinionay ofay emay, anyhow?ay”

Aay ittlelay overwhelmeday, Iay eganbay ethay eneralizedgay evasionsay ichwhay atthay
uestionqay eservesday.

ell“Way, I’may oinggay otay elltay ouyay omethingsay aboutay myay ife,lay” ehay interrupteday.
I“ay on’tday antway ouyay otay etgay aay ongwray ideaay ofay emay omfray allay esethay oriesstay ouyay
ear.hay”

Osay ehay asway awareay ofay ethay izarrebay accusationsay atthay avouredflay onversationcay
inay ishay allshay.

I’ll“ay elltay ouyay Od’sgay uth.tray” Ishay ightray andhay uddenlysay ordereday ivineday
etributionray otay andstay byay. I“ay amay ethay onsay ofay omesay ealthyway eoplepay inay ethay
Iddlemay Est—allway eadday ownay. Iay asway oughtbray upay inay Americaay utbay educateday atay
Oxforday, ecausebay allay myay ancestorsay avehay eenbay educateday erethay orfay anymay
earsyay. Itay isay aay amilyfay adition.tray”

Ehay ookedlay atay emay ideways—andsay Iay ewknay whyay Ordanjay Akerbay adhay elievedbay ehay
asway inglyay. Ehay urriedhay ethay asephray educated“ay atay Oxford,ay” oray allowedsway
itay, oray okedchay onay itay, asay oughthay itay adhay otheredbay imhay eforebay. Anday ithway
isthay oubtday, ishay olewhay atementstay ellfay otay iecespay, anday Iay onderedway ifay
erethay asn’tway omethingsay aay ittlelay inistersay aboutay imhay, afteray allay.

at“Whay artpay ofay ethay Iddlemay Est?way” Iay inquireday asuallycay.

an“Say Ancisco.fray”

I“ay ee.say”

“Myay amilyfay allay iedday anday Iay amecay intoay aay oodgay ealday ofay oney.may”

Ishay oicevay asway olemnsay, asay ifay ethay emorymay ofay atthay uddensay extinctionay ofay aay
anclay illstay auntedhay imhay. Orfay aay omentmay Iay uspectedsay atthay ehay asway ullingpay
myay eglay, utbay aay anceglay atay imhay onvincedcay emay otherwiseay.

After“ay atthay Iay ivedlay ikelay aay oungyay ajahray inay allay ethay apitalscay ofay
Europe—Parisay, Enicevay, Ome—collectingray ewelsjay, ieflychay ubiesray, untinghay
igbay amegay, aintingpay aay ittlelay, ingsthay orfay elfmysay onlyay, anday ingtryay otay
orgetfay omethingsay eryvay adsay atthay adhay appenedhay otay emay onglay ago.ay”

Ithway anay effortay Iay anagedmay otay estrainray myay incredulousay aughterlay. Ethay eryvay
asesphray ereway ornway osay eadbarethray atthay eythay evokeday onay imageay exceptay atthay
ofay aay urbanedtay aracter“chay” eakinglay awdustsay atay everyay orepay asay ehay ursuedpay
aay igertay oughthray ethay Oisbay eday Oulognebay.

en“Thay amecay ethay arway, olday ortspay. Itay asway aay eatgray eliefray, anday Iay iedtray eryvay
ardhay otay ieday, utbay Iay eemedsay otay earbay anay enchanteday ifelay. Iay accepteday aay
ommissioncay asay irstfay ieutenantlay enwhay itay eganbay. Inay ethay Argonneay Orestfay Iay
ooktay ethay emainsray ofay myay achine-gunmay attalionbay osay arfay orwardfay atthay erethay
asway aay alfhay ilemay apgay onay eitheray idesay ofay usay erewhay ethay infantryay ouldn’tcay
advanceay. Eway ayedstay erethay otway aysday anday otway ightsnay, aay undredhay anday irtythay
enmay ithway ixteensay Ewislay unsgay, anday enwhay ethay infantryay amecay upay atay astlay
eythay oundfay ethay insigniaay ofay eethray Ermangay ivisionsday amongay ethay ilespay ofay
eadday. Iay asway omotedpray otay ebay aay ajormay, anday everyay Allieday overnmentgay avegay
emay aay ecoration—evenday Ontenegromay, ittlelay Ontenegromay ownday onay ethay
Adriaticay Ea!say”

Ittlelay Ontenegromay! Ehay iftedlay upay ethay ordsway anday oddednay atay em—withthay ishay
ilesmay. Ethay ilesmay omprehendedcay Ontenegro’smay oubledtray istoryhay anday
athizedsympay ithway ethay avebray ugglesstray ofay ethay Ontenegrinmay eoplepay. Itay
appreciateday ullyfay ethay ainchay ofay ationalnay ircumstancescay ichwhay adhay
eliciteday isthay ibutetray omfray Ontenegro’smay armway ittlelay earthay. Myay
incredulityay asway ubmergedsay inay ascinationfay ownay; itay asway ikelay immingskay
astilyhay oughthray aay ozenday agazinesmay.

Ehay eachedray inay ishay ocketpay, anday aay iecepay ofay etalmay, ungslay onay aay ibbonray,
ellfay intoay myay almpay.

at’s“Thay ethay oneay omfray Ontenegro.may”

Otay myay astonishmentay, ethay ingthay adhay anay authenticay ooklay. Orderi“ay iday
Anilo,day” anray ethay ircularcay egendlay, ontenegro“May, Icolasnay Ex.ray”

urn“Tay it.ay”

ajor“May Ayjay Atsby,gay” Iay eadray, or“Fay Alourvay Extraordinary.ay”

ere’s“Hay anotheray ingthay Iay alwaysay arrycay. Aay ouvenirsay ofay Oxforday aysday. Itay
asway akentay inay Initytray Uad—theqay anmay onay myay eftlay isay ownay ethay Earlay ofay
Oncaster.day”

Itay asway aay otographphay ofay alfhay aay ozenday oungyay enmay inay azersblay oafinglay inay anay
archwayay oughthray ichwhay ereway isiblevay aay osthay ofay iresspay. Erethay asway Atsbygay,
ookinglay aay ittlelay, otnay uchmay, ounger—withyay aay icketcray atbay inay ishay andhay.

Enthay itay asway allay uetray. Iay awsay ethay insskay ofay igerstay amingflay inay ishay alacepay
onay ethay Andgray Analcay; Iay awsay imhay openingay aay estchay ofay ubiesray otay easeay, ithway
eirthay imson-lightedcray epthsday, ethay awingsgnay ofay ishay okenbray earthay.

I’m“ay oinggay otay akemay aay igbay equestray ofay ouyay oday,tay” ehay aidsay, ocketingpay ishay
ouvenirssay ithway atisfactionsay, o“say Iay oughtthay ouyay oughtay otay owknay omethingsay
aboutay emay. Iay idn’tday antway ouyay otay inkthay Iay asway ustjay omesay obodynay. Ouyay eesay,
Iay usuallyay indfay elfmysay amongay angersstray ecausebay Iay iftdray erehay anday erethay
ingtryay otay orgetfay ethay adsay ingsthay atthay appenedhay otay e.may” Ehay esitatedhay.
ou’ll“Yay earhay aboutay itay isthay afternoon.ay”

At“ay unch?lay”

o“Nay, isthay afternoonay. Iay appenedhay otay indfay outay atthay ou’reyay akingtay Issmay
Akerbay otay ea.tay”

o“Day ouyay eanmay ou’reyay inay ovelay ithway Issmay Aker?bay”

o“Nay, olday ortspay, I’may otnay. Utbay Issmay Akerbay ashay indlykay onsentedcay otay eakspay
otay ouyay aboutay isthay atter.may”

Iay adn’thay ethay aintestfay ideaay atwhay is“thay attermay” asway, utbay Iay asway oremay
annoyeday anthay interesteday. Iay adn’thay askeday Ordanjay otay eatay inay orderay otay
iscussday Mray. Ayjay Atsbygay. Iay asway uresay ethay equestray ouldway ebay omethingsay
utterlyay antasticfay, anday orfay aay omentmay Iay asway orrysay I’day everay etsay ootfay uponay
ishay overpopulateday awnlay.

Ehay ouldn’tway aysay anotheray ordway. Ishay orrectnesscay ewgray onay imhay asay eway earednay
ethay itycay. Eway assedpay Ortpay Ooseveltray, erewhay erethay asway aay impseglay ofay
ed-beltedray oceangoingay ipsshay, anday edspay alongay aay obbledcay umslay inedlay ithway
ethay arkday, undeserteday aloonssay ofay ethay aded-giltfay ineteen-hundredsnay.
Enthay ethay alleyvay ofay ashesay openeday outay onay othbay idessay ofay usay, anday Iay adhay aay
impseglay ofay Mrsay. Ilsonway ainingstray atay ethay aragegay umppay ithway antingpay
italityvay asay eway entway byay.

Ithway endersfay eadspray ikelay ingsway eway atteredscay ightlay oughthray alfhay
Astoria—onlyay alfhay, orfay asay eway istedtway amongay ethay illarspay ofay ethay elevateday
Iay eardhay ethay amiliarfay ug-jug-spat!“jay” ofay aay otorcyclemay, anday aay anticfray
olicemanpay oderay alongsideay.

All“ay ightray, olday ort,spay” alledcay Atsbygay. Eway owedslay ownday. Akingtay aay itewhay
ardcay omfray ishay alletway, ehay avedway itay eforebay ethay an’smay eyesay.

ight“Ray ouyay are,ay” agreeday ethay olicemanpay, ippingtay ishay apcay. ow“Knay ouyay extnay
imetay, Mray. Atsbygay. Excuseay e!may”

at“Whay asway at?thay” Iay inquireday. e“Thay icturepay ofay Oxford?ay”

I“ay asway ableay otay oday ethay ommissionercay aay avourfay onceay, anday ehay endssay emay aay
Istmaschray ardcay everyay ear.yay”

Overay ethay eatgray idgebray, ithway ethay unlightsay oughthray ethay irdersgay akingmay aay
onstantcay ickerflay uponay ethay ovingmay arscay, ithway ethay itycay isingray upay acrossay
ethay iverray inay itewhay eapshay anday ugarsay umpslay allay uiltbay ithway aay ishway outay ofay
onolfactorynay oneymay. Ethay itycay eensay omfray ethay Ueensboroqay Idgebray isay alwaysay
ethay itycay eensay orfay ethay irstfay imetay, inay itsay irstfay ildway omisepray ofay allay ethay
erymystay anday ethay eautybay inay ethay orldway.

Aay eadday anmay assedpay usay inay aay earsehay eapedhay ithway oomsblay, ollowedfay byay otway
arriagescay ithway awndray indsblay, anday byay oremay eerfulchay arriagescay orfay
iendsfray. Ethay iendsfray ookedlay outay atay usay ithway ethay agictray eyesay anday ortshay
upperay ipslay ofay outheasternsay Europeay, anday Iay asway adglay atthay ethay ightsay ofay
Atsby’sgay endidsplay arcay asway includeday inay eirthay ombresay olidayhay. Asay eway
ossedcray Ackwell’sblay Islanday aay imousinelay assedpay usay, ivendray byay aay itewhay
auffeurchay, inay ichwhay atsay eethray odishmay egroesnay, otway ucksbay anday aay irlgay. Iay
aughedlay alouday asay ethay olksyay ofay eirthay eyeballsay olledray owardtay usay inay
aughtyhay ivalryray.

Anything“ay ancay appenhay ownay atthay e’veway idslay overay isthay idge,bray” Iay oughtthay;
anything“ay atay allay …ay”

Evenay Atsbygay ouldcay appenhay, ithoutway anyay articularpay onderway.

Oaringray oonnay. Inay aay ell-fannedway Orty-secondfay Eetstray ellarcay Iay etmay Atsbygay
orfay unchlay. Inkingblay awayay ethay ightnessbray ofay ethay eetstray outsideay, myay eyesay
ickedpay imhay outay obscurelyay inay ethay anteroomay, alkingtay otay anotheray anmay.

“Mray. Arrawaycay, isthay isay myay iendfray Mray. Olfshiem.way”

Aay allsmay, at-nosedflay Ewjay aisedray ishay argelay eadhay anday egardedray emay ithway otway
inefay owthsgray ofay airhay ichwhay uxuriatedlay inay eitheray ostrilnay. Afteray aay
omentmay Iay iscoveredday ishay inytay eyesay inay ethay alf-darknesshay.

o“—Say Iay ooktay oneay ooklay atay im,hay” aidsay Mray. Olfshiemway, akingshay myay andhay
earnestlyay, and“ay atwhay oday ouyay inkthay Iay id?day”

at?“Whay” Iay inquireday olitelypay.

Utbay evidentlyay ehay asway otnay addressingay emay, orfay ehay oppeddray myay andhay anday
overedcay Atsbygay ithway ishay expressiveay osenay.

on’tday aypay imhay aay ennypay illtay ehay utsshay ishay outh.may’ Ehay utshay itay enthay anday
ere.thay”

Atsbygay ooktay anay armay ofay eachay ofay usay anday ovedmay orwardfay intoay ethay
estaurantray, ereuponwhay Mray. Olfshiemway allowedsway aay ewnay entencesay ehay asway
artingstay anday apsedlay intoay aay omnambulatorysay abstractionay.

ighballs?“Hay” askeday ethay eadhay aiterway.

etter!bay”

othay overay ere.thay”

ot“Hay anday all—yes,smay” aidsay Mray. Olfshiemway, ut“bay ullfay ofay emories.may”

at“Whay aceplay isay at?thay” Iay askeday.

e“Thay olday Etropole.may”

e“Thay olday Etropole,may” oodedbray Mray. Olfshiemway oomilyglay. illed“Fay ithway
acesfay eadday anday onegay. Illedfay ithway iendsfray onegay ownay oreverfay. Iay an’tcay
orgetfay osay onglay asay Iay ivelay ethay ightnay eythay otshay Osyray Osenthalray erethay. Itay
asway ixsay ofay usay atay ethay abletay, anday Osyray adhay eatay anday unkdray aay otlay allay

unnyfay ooklay anday ayssay omebodysay antsway otay eakspay otay imhay outsideay. All‘ay
ight,ray’ ayssay Osyray, anday eginsbay otay etgay upay, anday Iay ulledpay imhay ownday inay ishay
airchay.

“ et‘Lay ethay astardsbay omecay inay erehay ifay eythay antway ouyay, Osyray, utbay on’tday
ouyay, osay elphay emay, ovemay outsideay isthay oom.ray’

indsblay e’dway ofay eensay aylight.day”

id“Day ehay o?gay” Iay askeday innocentlyay.

ure“Say ehay ent.way” Mray. Olfshiem’sway osenay ashedflay atay emay indignantlyay. e“Hay

Oh!“ay”

I’ve“ay eardhay ofay it.ay”

inest“Fay ecimensspay ofay umanhay olars,may” ehay informeday emay.

A“ay entist?day”

ouldway avehay oughtthay ofay itay asay aay ingthay atthay erelymay appenedhay, ethay enday ofay

ingle-mindednesssay ofay aay urglarbay owingblay aay afesay.

ey“Thay an’tcay etgay imhay, olday ortspay. E’shay aay artsmay an.may”

aughtcay ightsay ofay Omtay Uchananbay acrossay ethay owdedcray oomray.

ome“Cay alongay ithway emay orfay aay inute,may” Iay aidsay; I’ve“ay otgay otay aysay ellohay otay
omeone.say”

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Oneay Octoberay ayday inay ineteen-seventeennay—

aid(say Ordanjay Akerbay atthay afternoonay, ittingsay upay eryvay aightstray onay aay
aightstray airchay inay ethay ea-gardentay atay ethay Azaplay Otelhay)

I—ay asway alkingway alongay omfray oneay aceplay otay anotheray, alfhay onay ethay idewalkssay
anday alfhay onay ethay awnslay. Iay asway appierhay onay ethay awnslay ecausebay Iay adhay onay
oesshay omfray Englanday ithway ubberray obsknay onay ethay olessay atthay itbay intoay ethay
oftsay oundgray. Iay adhay onay aay ewnay aidplay irtskay alsoay atthay ewblay aay ittlelay inay ethay
indway, anday eneverwhay isthay appenedhay ethay edray, itewhay, anday ueblay annersbay inay
ontfray ofay allay ethay ouseshay etchedstray outay iffstay anday aidsay ut-tut-tut-tuttay,
inay aay isapprovingday ayway.

Ethay argestlay ofay ethay annersbay anday ethay argestlay ofay ethay awnslay elongedbay otay
Aisyday Ay’sfay ousehay. Eshay asway ustjay eighteenay, otway earsyay olderay anthay emay, anday
byay arfay ethay ostmay opularpay ofay allay ethay oungyay irlsgay inay Ouisvillelay. Eshay
esseddray inay itewhay, anday adhay aay ittlelay itewhay oadsterray, anday allay ayday onglay
ethay elephonetay angray inay erhay ousehay anday exciteday oungyay officersay omfray Ampcay
Aylortay emandedday ethay ivilegepray ofay onopolizingmay erhay atthay
ightnay. Anyways“ay, orfay anay our!hay”

Enwhay Iay amecay oppositeay erhay ousehay atthay orningmay erhay itewhay oadsterray asway
esidebay ethay erbkay, anday eshay asway ittingsay inay itay ithway aay ieutenantlay Iay adhay
evernay eensay eforebay. Eythay ereway osay engrosseday inay eachay otheray atthay eshay
idn’tday eesay emay untilay Iay asway ivefay eetfay awayay.

ello“Hay, Ordan,jay” eshay alledcay unexpectedlyay. ease“Play omecay ere.hay”

Iay asway atteredflay atthay eshay antedway otay eakspay otay emay, ecausebay ofay allay ethay
olderay irlsgay Iay admireday erhay ostmay. Eshay askeday emay ifay Iay asway oinggay otay ethay Edray
Osscray otay akemay andagesbay. Iay asway. Ellway, enthay, ouldway Iay elltay emthay atthay eshay
ouldn’tcay omecay atthay ayday? Ethay officeray ookedlay atay Aisyday ilewhay eshay asway
eakingspay, inay aay ayway atthay everyay oungyay irlgay antsway otay ebay ookedlay atay
ometimesay, anday ecausebay itay eemedsay omanticray otay emay Iay avehay ememberedray ethay
incidentay everay incesay. Ishay amenay asway Ayjay Atsbygay, anday Iay idn’tday aylay eyesay onay
imhay againay orfay overay ourfay ears—evenyay afteray I’day etmay imhay onay Onglay Islanday Iay
idn’tday ealizeray itay asway ethay amesay anmay.

Atthay asway ineteen-seventeennay. Byay ethay extnay earyay Iay adhay aay ewfay eauxbay
elfmysay, anday Iay eganbay otay ayplay inay ournamentstay, osay Iay idn’tday eesay Aisyday eryvay
oftenay. Eshay entway ithway aay ightlyslay olderay owd—whencray eshay entway ithway anyoneay
atay allay. Ildway umoursray ereway irculatingcay aboutay er—howhay erhay othermay adhay
oundfay erhay ackingpay erhay agbay oneay interway ightnay otay ogay otay Ewnay Orkyay anday aysay
oodbyegay otay aay oldiersay owhay asway oinggay overseasay. Eshay asway effectuallyay
eventedpray, utbay eshay asn’tway onay eakingspay ermstay ithway erhay amilyfay orfay
everalsay eeksway. Afteray atthay eshay idn’tday ayplay arounday ithway ethay oldierssay anyay
oremay, utbay onlyay ithway aay ewfay at-footedflay, ortsightedshay oungyay enmay inay owntay,
owhay ouldn’tcay etgay intoay ethay armyay atay allay.

Byay ethay extnay autumnay eshay asway aygay againay, aygay asay everay. Eshay adhay aay utdébay
afteray ethay armisticeay, anday inay Ebruaryfay eshay asway esumablypray engageday otay aay
anmay omfray Ewnay Orleansay. Inay Unejay eshay arriedmay Omtay Uchananbay ofay Icagochay,
ithway oremay omppay anday ircumstancecay anthay Ouisvillelay everay ewknay eforebay. Ehay
amecay ownday ithway aay undredhay eoplepay inay ourfay ivatepray arscay, anday iredhay aay
olewhay oorflay ofay ethay Uhlbachmay Otelhay, anday ethay ayday eforebay ethay eddingway ehay
avegay erhay aay ingstray ofay earlspay aluedvay atay eethray undredhay anday iftyfay ousandthay
ollarsday.

Iay asway aay idesmaidbray. Iay amecay intoay erhay oomray alfhay anay ourhay eforebay ethay
idalbray innerday, anday oundfay erhay inglyay onay erhay edbay asay ovelylay asay ethay Unejay
ightnay inay erhay oweredflay ess—anddray asay unkdray asay aay onkeymay. Eshay adhay aay ottlebay
ofay Auternesay inay oneay andhay anday aay etterlay inay ethay otheray.

“ atulate’Gray e,may” eshay utteredmay. ever“Nay adhay aay inkdray eforebay, utbay ohay owhay
Iay oday enjoyay it.ay”

at’s“Whay ethay attermay, Aisy?day”

Iay asway aredscay, Iay ancay elltay ouyay; I’day evernay eensay aay irlgay ikelay atthay eforebay.

ere“Hay, earies.day” Eshay opedgray arounday inay aay astebasketway eshay adhay ithway erhay
onay ethay edbay anday ulledpay outay ethay ingstray ofay earlspay. ake“Tay em’ay ownstairsday
anday ivegay em’ay ackbay otay oeverwhay eythay elongbay otay. Elltay em’ay allay Aisy’sday
angechay’ erhay inemay. Aysay: aisy’s‘Day angechay’ erhay ine!may’ ”

Eshay eganbay otay ecry—shay iedcray anday iedcray. Iay ushedray outay anday oundfay erhay
other’smay aidmay, anday eway ockedlay ethay oorday anday otgay erhay intoay aay oldcay athbay.
Eshay ouldn’tway etlay ogay ofay ethay etterlay. Eshay ooktay itay intoay ethay ubtay ithway erhay
anday ueezedsqay itay upay inay aay etway allbay, anday onlyay etlay emay eavelay itay inay ethay
oap-dishsay enwhay eshay awsay atthay itay asway omingcay otay iecespay ikelay owsnay.

Utbay eshay idn’tday aysay anotheray ordway. Eway avegay erhay iritsspay ofay ammoniaay anday
utpay iceay onay erhay oreheadfay anday ookedhay erhay ackbay intoay erhay essdray, anday alfhay
anay ourhay aterlay, enwhay eway alkedway outay ofay ethay oomray, ethay earlspay ereway arounday
erhay ecknay anday ethay incidentay asway overay. Extnay ayday atay ivefay o’clockay eshay
arriedmay Omtay Uchananbay ithoutway osay uchmay asay aay ivershay, anday artedstay offay onay aay
eethray onthsmay’ iptray otay ethay Outhsay Eassay.

Iay awsay emthay inay Antasay Arbarabay enwhay eythay amecay ackbay, anday Iay oughtthay I’day
evernay eensay aay irlgay osay admay aboutay erhay usbandhay. Ifay ehay eftlay ethay oomray orfay aay
inutemay e’dshay ooklay arounday uneasilyay, anday aysay: ere’s“Whay Omtay one?gay” anday
earway ethay ostmay abstracteday expressionay untilay eshay awsay imhay omingcay inay ethay
oorday. Eshay useday otay itsay onay ethay andsay ithway ishay eadhay inay erhay aplay byay ethay
ourhay, ubbingray erhay ingersfay overay ishay eyesay anday ookinglay atay imhay ithway
unfathomableay elightday. Itay asway ouchingtay otay eesay emthay ogether—ittay ademay ouyay
aughlay inay aay ushedhay, ascinatedfay ayway. Atthay asway inay Augustay. Aay eekway afteray Iay
eftlay Antasay Arbarabay Omtay anray intoay aay agonway onay ethay Enturavay oadray oneay ightnay,
anday ippedray aay ontfray eelwhay offay ishay arcay. Ethay irlgay owhay asway ithway imhay otgay
intoay ethay aperspay, ootay, ecausebay erhay armay asway oken—shebray asway oneay ofay ethay
ambermaidschay inay ethay Antasay Arbarabay Otelhay.

Ethay extnay Aprilay Aisyday adhay erhay ittlelay irlgay, anday eythay entway otay Ancefray orfay
aay earyay. Iay awsay emthay oneay ingspray inay Annescay, anday aterlay inay Eauvilleday, anday
enthay eythay amecay ackbay otay Icagochay otay ettlesay ownday. Aisyday asway opularpay inay
Icagochay, asay ouyay owknay. Eythay ovedmay ithway aay astfay owdcray, allay ofay emthay oungyay
anday ichray anday ildway, utbay eshay amecay outay ithway anay absolutelyay erfectpay
eputationray. Erhapspay ecausebay eshay oesn’tday inkdray. It’say aay eatgray advantageay
otnay otay inkdray amongay ard-drinkinghay eoplepay. Ouyay ancay oldhay ouryay onguetay anday,
oreovermay, ouyay ancay imetay anyay ittlelay irregularityay ofay ouryay ownay osay atthay
everybodyay elseay isay osay indblay atthay eythay on’tday eesay oray arecay. Erhapspay Aisyday
evernay entway inay orfay amouray atay all—anday etyay ere’sthay omethingsay inay atthay oicevay
ofay ershay …

Ellway, aboutay ixsay eeksway agoay, eshay eardhay ethay amenay Atsbygay orfay ethay irstfay
imetay inay earsyay. Itay asway enwhay Iay askeday ou—doyay ouyay emember?—ifray ouyay ewknay
Atsbygay inay Estway Eggay. Afteray ouyay adhay onegay omehay eshay amecay intoay myay oomray anday
okeway emay upay, anday aidsay: at“Whay Atsby?gay” anday enwhay Iay escribedday im—Ihay asway
alfhay asleep—sheay aidsay inay ethay angeststray oicevay atthay itay ustmay ebay ethay anmay
eshay useday otay owknay. Itay asn’tway untilay enthay atthay Iay onnectedcay isthay Atsbygay
ithway ethay officeray inay erhay itewhay arcay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Enwhay Ordanjay Akerbay adhay inishedfay ellingtay allay isthay eway adhay eftlay ethay Azaplay
orfay alfhay anay ourhay anday ereway ivingdray inay aay ictoriavay oughthray Entralcay Arkpay.
Ethay unsay adhay onegay ownday ehindbay ethay alltay apartmentsay ofay ethay oviemay arsstay inay
ethay Estway Iftiesfay, anday ethay earclay oicesvay ofay ildrenchay, alreadyay atheredgay
ikelay icketscray onay ethay assgray, oseray oughthray ethay othay ilighttway:

I’m“ay ethay Eikshay ofay Arabyay. Ouryay ovelay elongsbay otay emay. Atay ightnay enwhay
ou’reyay asleepay Intoay ouryay enttay I’llay eep—cray”

It“ay asway aay angestray oincidence,cay” Iay aidsay.

ut“Bay itay asn’tway aay oincidencecay atay all.ay”

“Whyay ot?nay”

atsby“Gay oughtbay atthay ousehay osay atthay Aisyday ouldway ebay ustjay acrossay ethay ay.bay”

Oh!“ay”

oes“Day eshay antway otay eesay Atsby?gay”

e’s“Shay otnay otay owknay aboutay itay. Atsbygay oesn’tday antway erhay otay owknay. Ou’reyay
ustjay upposedsay otay inviteay erhay otay ea.tay”

Eway assedpay aay arrierbay ofay arkday eestray, anday enthay ethay açadefay ofay Ifty-Ninthfay

Vay

Enwhay Iay amecay omehay otay Estway Eggay atthay ightnay Iay asway afraiday orfay aay omentmay atthay
myay ousehay asway onay irefay. Otway o’clockay anday ethay olewhay ornercay ofay ethay
eninsulapay asway azingblay ithway ightlay, ichwhay ellfay unrealay onay ethay ubberyshray
anday ademay inthay elongatingay intsglay uponay ethay oadsideray iresway. Urningtay aay
ornercay, Iay awsay atthay itay asway Atsby’sgay ousehay, itlay omfray owertay otay ellarcay.

Atay irstfay Iay oughtthay itay asway anotheray artypay, aay ildway outray atthay adhay esolvedray
itselfay intoay ide-and-go-seek“hay” oray ardines-in-the-box“say” ithway allay ethay
ousehay ownthray openay otay ethay amegay. Utbay erethay asn’tway aay oundsay. Onlyay indway inay
ethay eestray, ichwhay ewblay ethay iresway anday ademay ethay ightslay ogay offay anday onay
againay asay ifay ethay ousehay adhay inkedway intoay ethay arknessday. Asay myay axitay oanedgray
awayay Iay awsay Atsbygay alkingway owardtay emay acrossay ishay awnlay.

our“Yay aceplay ookslay ikelay ethay Orld’sway Air,fay” Iay aidsay.

ell“Way, isthay ouldway interestay ouyay. Itay ouldn’tway aketay upay uchmay ofay ouryay imetay

on’t“Day ingbray Om,tay” Iay arnedway erhay.

at?“Whay”

on’t“Day ingbray Om.tay”

o“Whay isay om’?‘Tay” eshay askeday innocentlyay.

Ethay ayday agreeday uponay asway ouringpay ainray. Atay elevenay o’clockay aay anmay inay aay
aincoatray, aggingdray aay awn-mowerlay, appedtay atay myay ontfray oorday anday aidsay atthay
Mray. Atsbygay adhay entsay imhay overay otay utcay myay assgray. Isthay emindedray emay atthay Iay
adhay orgottenfay otay elltay myay Innfay otay omecay ackbay, osay Iay ovedray intoay Estway Eggay
Illagevay otay earchsay orfay erhay amongay oggysay itewashedwhay alleysay anday otay uybay
omesay upscay anday emonslay anday owersflay.

Ethay owersflay ereway unnecessaryay, orfay atay otway o’clockay aay eenhousegray arriveday
omfray Atsby’sgay, ithway innumerableay eceptaclesray otay ontaincay itay. Anay ourhay
aterlay ethay ontfray oorday openeday ervouslynay, anday Atsbygay inay aay itewhay annelflay
uitsay, ilversay irtshay, anday old-colouredgay ietay, urriedhay inay. Ehay asway alepay,
anday erethay ereway arkday ignssay ofay eeplessnessslay eneathbay ishay eyesay.

Is“ay everythingay allay ight?ray” ehay askeday immediatelyay.

e“Thay assgray ookslay inefay, ifay at’sthay atwhay ouyay ean.may”

at“Whay ass?gray” ehay inquireday anklyblay. Oh“ay, ethay assgray inay ethay ard.yay” Ehay
ookedlay outay ethay indowway atay itay, utbay, udgingjay omfray ishay expressionay, Iay on’tday
elievebay ehay awsay aay ingthay.

ooks“Lay eryvay ood,gay” ehay emarkedray aguelyvay. One“ay ofay ethay aperspay aidsay eythay
oughtthay ethay ainray ouldway opstay aboutay ourfay. Iay inkthay itay asway Ethay

Iay ooktay imhay intoay ethay antrypay, erewhay ehay ookedlay aay ittlelay eproachfullyray atay
ethay Innfay. Ogethertay eway utinizedscray ethay elvetway emonlay akescay omfray ethay
elicatessenday opshay.

ill“Way eythay o?day” Iay askeday.

Of“ay oursecay, ofay oursecay! Ey’rethay ine!fay” anday ehay addeday ollowlyhay, “ay… olday
ort.spay”

Ethay ainray ooledcay aboutay alf-pasthay eethray otay aay ampday istmay, oughthray ichwhay
occasionalay inthay opsdray amsway ikelay ewday. Atsbygay ookedlay ithway acantvay eyesay

imetay otay imetay asay ifay aay eriessay ofay invisibleay utbay alarmingay appeningshay ereway
akingtay aceplay outsideay. Inallyfay ehay otgay upay anday informeday emay, inay anay
uncertainay oicevay, atthay ehay asway oinggay omehay.

“Why’say at?thay”

obody’s“Nay omingcay otay eatay. It’say ootay ate!lay” Ehay ookedlay atay ishay atchway asay ifay

allay ay.day”

on’t“Day ebay illysay; it’say ustjay otway inutesmay otay our.fay”

Ehay atsay ownday iserablymay, asay ifay Iay adhay ushedpay imhay, anday imultaneouslysay

Underay ethay ippingdray arebay ilac-treeslay aay argelay openay arcay asway omingcay upay ethay
ivedray. Itay oppedstay. Aisy’sday acefay, ippedtay idewayssay eneathbay aay
ee-corneredthray avenderlay athay, ookedlay outay atay emay ithway aay ightbray ecstaticay

Is“ay isthay absolutelyay erewhay ouyay ivelay, myay earestday one?ay”

Ethay exhilaratingay ippleray ofay erhay oicevay asway aay ildway onictay inay ethay ainray. Iay
adhay otay ollowfay ethay oundsay ofay itay orfay aay omentmay, upay anday ownday, ithway myay earay
aloneay, eforebay anyay ordsway amecay oughthray. Aay ampday eakstray ofay airhay aylay ikelay aay

isteningglay opsdray asay Iay ooktay itay otay elphay erhay omfray ethay arcay.

Are“ay ouyay inay ovelay ithway e,may” eshay aidsay owlay inay myay earay, or“ay whyay idday Iay avehay
otay omecay alone?ay”

awayay anday endspay anay our.hay”

ome“Cay ackbay inay anay ourhay, Erdie.fay” Enthay inay aay avegray urmurmay: is“Hay amenay isay
Erdie.fay”

oes“Day ethay asolinegay affectay ishay ose?nay”

I“ay on’tday inkthay o,say” eshay aidsay innocentlyay. “Why?ay”

Eway entway inay. Otay myay overwhelmingay urprisesay ethay iving-roomlay asway esertedday.

ell“Way, at’sthay unny,fay” Iay exclaimeday.

at’s“Whay unny?fay”

Eshay urnedtay erhay eadhay asay erethay asway aay ightlay ignifiedday ockingknay atay ethay
ontfray oorday. Iay entway outay anday openeday itay. Atsbygay, alepay asay eathday, ithway ishay
andshay ungedplay ikelay eightsway inay ishay oatcay ocketspay, asway andingstay inay aay
uddlepay ofay aterway aringglay agicallytray intoay myay eyesay.

Ithway ishay andshay illstay inay ishay oatcay ocketspay ehay alkedstay byay emay intoay ethay
allhay, urnedtay arplyshay asay ifay ehay ereway onay aay ireway, anday isappearedday intoay ethay
iving-roomlay. Itay asn’tway aay itbay unnyfay. Awareay ofay ethay oudlay eatingbay ofay myay
ownay earthay Iay ulledpay ethay oorday otay againstay ethay increasingay ainray.

Orfay alfhay aay inutemay erethay asn’tway aay oundsay. Enthay omfray ethay iving-roomlay Iay
eardhay aay ortsay ofay okingchay urmurmay anday artpay ofay aay aughlay, ollowedfay byay
Aisy’sday oicevay onay aay earclay artificialay otenay:

I“ay ertainlycay amay awfullyay adglay otay eesay ouyay again.ay”

Aay ausepay; itay endureday orriblyhay. Iay adhay othingnay otay oday inay ethay allhay, osay Iay
entway intoay ethay oomray.

Atsbygay, ishay andshay illstay inay ishay ocketspay, asway ecliningray againstay ethay
antelpiecemay inay aay ainedstray ounterfeitcay ofay erfectpay easeay, evenay ofay
oredombay. Ishay eadhay eanedlay ackbay osay arfay atthay itay estedray againstay ethay acefay
ofay aay efunctday antelpiecemay ockclay, anday omfray isthay ositionpay ishay istraughtday
eyesay aredstay ownday atay Aisyday, owhay asway ittingsay, ightenedfray utbay acefulgray,
onay ethay edgeay ofay aay iffstay airchay.

e’ve“Way etmay efore,bay” utteredmay Atsbygay. Ishay eyesay ancedglay omentarilymay atay
emay, anday ishay ipslay artedpay ithway anay abortiveay attemptay atay aay aughlay. Uckilylay
ethay ockclay ooktay isthay omentmay otay ilttay angerouslyday atay ethay essurepray ofay ishay
eadhay, ereuponwhay ehay urnedtay anday aughtcay itay ithway emblingtray ingersfay, anday
etsay itay ackbay inay aceplay. Enthay ehay atsay ownday, igidlyray, ishay elboway onay ethay armay
ofay ethay ofasay anday ishay inchay inay ishay andhay.

I’m“ay orrysay aboutay ethay ock,clay” ehay aidsay.

Myay ownay acefay adhay ownay assumeday aay eepday opicaltray urnbay. Iay ouldn’tcay ustermay upay
aay inglesay ommonplacecay outay ofay ethay ousandthay inay myay eadhay.

It’s“ay anay olday ock,clay” Iay oldtay emthay idioticallyay.

Iay inkthay eway allay elievedbay orfay aay omentmay atthay itay adhay ashedsmay inay iecespay onay
ethay oorflay.

e“Way aven’thay etmay orfay anymay ears,yay” aidsay Aisyday, erhay oicevay asay
atter-of-factmay asay itay ouldcay everay ebay.

ive“Fay earsyay extnay Ovember.nay”

Ethay automaticay ualityqay ofay Atsby’sgay answeray etsay usay allay ackbay atay eastlay
anotheray inutemay. Iay adhay emthay othbay onay eirthay eetfay ithway ethay esperateday
uggestionsay atthay eythay elphay emay akemay eatay inay ethay itchenkay enwhay ethay emoniacday
Innfay oughtbray itay inay onay aay aytray.

Amiday ethay elcomeway onfusioncay ofay upscay anday akescay aay ertaincay icalphysay
ecencyday establisheday itselfay. Atsbygay otgay imselfhay intoay aay adowshay anday,
ilewhay Aisyday anday Iay alkedtay, ookedlay onscientiouslycay omfray oneay otay ethay otheray
ofay usay ithway ensetay, unhappyay eyesay. Oweverhay, asay almnesscay asn’tway anay enday inay
itselfay, Iay ademay anay excuseay atay ethay irstfay ossiblepay omentmay, anday otgay otay myay
eetfay.

ere“Whay areay ouyay oing?gay” emandedday Atsbygay inay immediateay alarmay.

I’ll“ay ebay ack.bay”

I’ve“ay otgay otay eakspay otay ouyay aboutay omethingsay eforebay ouyay o.gay”

Ehay ollowedfay emay ildlyway intoay ethay itchenkay, osedclay ethay oorday, anday

at’s“Whay ethay atter?may”
