e’s“Shay embarrassed?ay” ehay epeatedray incredulouslyay.

ust“Jay asay uchmay asay ouyay are.ay”

on’t“Day alktay osay oud.lay”

ou’re“Yay actingay ikelay aay ittlelay oy,bay” Iay okebray outay impatientlyay. ot“Nay onlyay
atthay, utbay ou’reyay uderay. Aisy’sday ittingsay inay erethay allay alone.ay”

Ehay aisedray ishay andhay otay opstay myay ordsway, ookedlay atay emay ithway unforgettableay
eproachray, anday, openingay ethay oorday autiouslycay, entway ackbay intoay ethay otheray
oomray.

Iay alkedway outay ethay ackbay ay—justway asay Atsbygay adhay enwhay ehay adhay ademay ishay
ervousnay ircuitcay ofay ethay ousehay alfhay anay ourhay efore—andbay anray orfay aay ugehay
ackblay ottedknay eetray, osewhay assedmay eaveslay ademay aay abricfay againstay ethay
ainray. Onceay oremay itay asway ouringpay, anday myay irregularay awnlay, ell-shavedway byay
Atsby’sgay ardenergay, aboundeday inay allsmay uddymay ampssway anday ehistoricpray
arshesmay. Erethay asway othingnay otay ooklay atay omfray underay ethay eetray exceptay
Atsby’sgay enormousay ousehay, osay Iay aredstay atay itay, ikelay Antkay atay ishay urchchay
eeplestay, orfay alfhay anay ourhay. Aay ewerbray adhay uiltbay itay earlyay inay ethay eriod“pay”
azecray, aay ecadeday eforebay, anday erethay asway aay orystay atthay e’dhay agreeday otay aypay
ivefay earsyay’ axestay onay allay ethay eighbouringnay ottagescay ifay ethay ownersay ouldway
avehay eirthay oofsray atchedthay ithway awstray. Erhapspay eirthay efusalray ooktay ethay
earthay outay ofay ishay anplay otay Oundfay aay Amily—hefay entway intoay anay immediateay
eclineday. Ishay ildrenchay oldsay ishay ousehay ithway ethay ackblay eathwray illstay onay
ethay oorday. Americansay, ilewhay illingway, evenay eageray, otay ebay erfssay, avehay
alwaysay eenbay obstinateay aboutay eingbay easantrypay.

Afteray alfhay anay ourhay, ethay unsay oneshay againay, anday ethay ocer’sgray automobileay
oundedray Atsby’sgay ivedray ithway ethay awray aterialmay orfay ishay ervantssay’
inner—Iday eltfay uresay ehay ouldn’tway eatay aay oonfulspay. Aay aidmay eganbay openingay
ethay upperay indowsway ofay ishay ousehay, appeareday omentarilymay inay eachay, anday,
eaninglay omfray ethay argelay entralcay aybay, atspay editativelymay intoay ethay
ardengay. Itay asway imetay Iay entway ackbay. Ilewhay ethay ainray ontinuedcay itay adhay
eemedsay ikelay ethay urmurmay ofay eirthay oicesvay, isingray anday ellingsway aay ittlelay
ownay anday enthay ithway ustsgay ofay emotionay. Utbay inay ethay ewnay ilencesay Iay eltfay atthay
ilencesay adhay allenfay ithinway ethay ousehay ootay.

Iay entway in—afteray akingmay everyay ossiblepay oisenay inay ethay itchenkay, ortshay ofay
ushingpay overay ethay ove—butstay Iay on’tday elievebay eythay eardhay aay oundsay. Eythay
ereway ittingsay atay eitheray enday ofay ethay ouchcay, ookinglay atay eachay otheray asay ifay
omesay uestionqay adhay eenbay askeday, oray asway inay ethay airay, anday everyay estigevay ofay
embarrassmentay asway onegay. Aisy’sday acefay asway earedsmay ithway earstay, anday enwhay
Iay amecay inay eshay umpedjay upay anday eganbay ipingway atay itay ithway erhay andkerchiefhay
eforebay aay irrormay. Utbay erethay asway aay angechay inay Atsbygay atthay asway implysay
onfoundingcay. Ehay iterallylay owedglay; ithoutway aay ordway oray aay esturegay ofay
exultationay aay ewnay ell-beingway adiatedray omfray imhay anday illedfay ethay ittlelay
oomray.

Oh“ay, ellohay, olday ort,spay” ehay aidsay, asay ifay ehay adn’thay eensay emay orfay earsyay. Iay
oughtthay orfay aay omentmay ehay asway oinggay otay akeshay andshay.

It’s“ay oppedstay aining.ray”

as“Hay it?ay” Enwhay ehay ealizedray atwhay Iay asway alkingtay aboutay, atthay erethay ereway
inkle-bellstway ofay unshinesay inay ethay oomray, ehay iledsmay ikelay aay eatherway anmay,
ikelay anay ecstaticay atronpay ofay ecurrentray ightlay, anday epeatedray ethay ewsnay otay
Aisyday. at“Whay oday ouyay inkthay ofay atthay? It’say oppedstay aining.ray”

I’m“ay adglay, Ay.jay” Erhay oatthray, ullfay ofay achingay, ievinggray eautybay, oldtay
onlyay ofay erhay unexpecteday oyjay.

I“ay antway ouyay anday Aisyday otay omecay overay otay myay ouse,hay” ehay aidsay, I’d“ay ikelay otay
owshay erhay around.ay”

ou’re“Yay uresay ouyay antway emay otay ome?cay”

Absolutely“ay, olday ort.spay”

Aisyday entway upstairsay otay ashway erhay ace—toofay atelay Iay oughtthay ithway
umiliationhay ofay myay owels—whiletay Atsbygay anday Iay aitedway onay ethay awnlay.

“Myay ousehay ookslay ellway, oesn’tday it?ay” ehay emandedday. ee“Say owhay ethay olewhay
ontfray ofay itay atchescay ethay ight.lay”

Iay agreeday atthay itay asway endidsplay.

es.“Yay” Ishay eyesay entway overay itay, everyay archeday oorday anday uaresqay owertay. It“ay
ooktay emay ustjay eethray earsyay otay earnay ethay oneymay atthay oughtbay it.ay”

I“ay oughtthay ouyay inheriteday ouryay oney.may”

I“ay idday, olday ort,spay” ehay aidsay automaticallyay, ut“bay Iay ostlay ostmay ofay itay inay
ethay igbay anic—thepay anicpay ofay ethay ar.way”

Iay inkthay ehay ardlyhay ewknay atwhay ehay asway ayingsay, orfay enwhay Iay askeday imhay atwhay
usinessbay ehay asway inay ehay answereday: at’s“Thay myay affair,ay” eforebay ehay ealizedray
atthay itay asn’tway anay appropriateay eplyray.

Oh“ay, I’veay eenbay inay everalsay ings,thay” ehay orrectedcay imselfhay. I“ay asway inay ethay
ugdray usinessbay anday enthay Iay asway inay ethay oilay usinessbay. Utbay I’may otnay inay
eitheray oneay ow.nay” Ehay ookedlay atay emay ithway oremay attentionay. o“Day ouyay eanmay
ou’veyay eenbay inkingthay overay atwhay Iay oposedpray ethay otheray ight?nay”

Eforebay Iay ouldcay answeray, Aisyday amecay outay ofay ethay ousehay anday otway owsray ofay
assbray uttonsbay onay erhay essdray eamedglay inay ethay unlightsay.

at“Thay ugehay aceplay ere?thay” eshay iedcray ointingpay.

o“Day ouyay ikelay it?ay”

I“ay ovelay itay, utbay Iay on’tday eesay owhay ouyay ivelay erethay allay alone.ay”

I“ay eepkay itay alwaysay ullfay ofay interestingay eoplepay, ightnay anday ayday. Eoplepay
owhay oday interestingay ingsthay. Elebratedcay eople.pay”

Insteaday ofay akingtay ethay ortcutshay alongay ethay Oundsay eway entway ownday otay ethay
oadray anday entereday byay ethay igbay osternpay. Ithway enchantingay urmursmay Aisyday
admireday isthay aspectay oray atthay ofay ethay eudalfay ilhouettesay againstay ethay skyay,
admireday ethay ardensgay, ethay arklingspay odouray ofay onquilsjay anday ethay othyfray
odouray ofay awthornhay anday umplay ossomsblay anday ethay alepay oldgay odouray ofay
iss-me-at-the-gatekay. Itay asway angestray otay eachray ethay arblemay epsstay anday indfay
onay irstay ofay ightbray essesdray inay anday outay ethay oorday, anday earhay onay oundsay utbay
irdbay oicesvay inay ethay eestray.

Anday insideay, asay eway anderedway oughthray Ariemay Antoinetteay usic-roomsmay anday
Estorationray Alonssay, Iay eltfay atthay erethay ereway uestsgay oncealedcay ehindbay
everyay ouchcay anday abletay, underay ordersay otay ebay eathlesslybray ilentsay untilay eway
adhay assedpay oughthray. Asay Atsbygay osedclay ethay oorday ofay e“thay Ertonmay Ollegecay
Ibrarylay” Iay ouldcay avehay ornsway Iay eardhay ethay owl-eyeday anmay eakbray intoay
ostlyghay aughterlay.

Eway entway upstairsay, oughthray eriodpay edroomsbay athedsway inay oseray anday avenderlay
ilksay anday ividvay ithway ewnay owersflay, oughthray essing-roomsdray anday oolroomspay,
anday athroomsbay ithway unkensay aths—intrudingbay intoay oneay amberchay erewhay aay
ishevelledday anmay inay amaspyjay asway oingday iverlay exercisesay onay ethay oorflay. Itay
asway Mray. Ipspringerklay, ethay oarder.“bay” Iay adhay eensay imhay anderingway ungrilyhay
aboutay ethay eachbay atthay orningmay. Inallyfay eway amecay otay Atsby’sgay ownay
apartmentay, aay edroombay anday aay athbay, anday anay Adam’say udystay, erewhay eway atsay
ownday anday ankdray aay assglay ofay omesay Artreusechay ehay ooktay omfray aay upboardcay inay
ethay allway.

Ehay adn’thay onceay easedcay ookinglay atay Aisyday, anday Iay inkthay ehay evaluedray
everythingay inay ishay ousehay accordingay otay ethay easuremay ofay esponseray itay ewdray
omfray erhay ell-lovedway eyesay. Ometimessay ootay, ehay aredstay arounday atay ishay
ossessionspay inay aay azedday ayway, asay oughthay inay erhay actualay anday astoundingay
esencepray onenay ofay itay asway anyay ongerlay ealray. Onceay ehay earlynay oppledtay ownday aay
ightflay ofay airsstay.

Ishay edroombay asway ethay implestsay oomray ofay all—exceptay erewhay ethay esserdray asway
arnishedgay ithway aay oilettay etsay ofay urepay ullday oldgay. Aisyday ooktay ethay ushbray
ithway elightday, anday oothedsmay erhay airhay, ereuponwhay Atsbygay atsay ownday anday
adedshay ishay eyesay anday eganbay otay aughlay.

It’s“ay ethay unniestfay ingthay, olday ort,spay” ehay aidsay ilariouslyhay. I“ay
an’t—Whencay Iay tryay o—tay”

Ehay adhay assedpay isiblyvay oughthray otway atesstay anday asway enteringay uponay aay
irdthay. Afteray ishay embarrassmentay anday ishay unreasoningay oyjay ehay asway onsumedcay
ithway onderway atay erhay esencepray. Ehay adhay eenbay ullfay ofay ethay ideaay osay onglay,
eameddray itay ightray oughthray otay ethay enday, aitedway ithway ishay eethtay etsay, osay otay
eakspay, atay anay inconceivableay itchpay ofay intensityay. Ownay, inay ethay eactionray,
ehay asway unningray ownday ikelay anay over-wounday ockclay.

Ecoveringray imselfhay inay aay inutemay ehay openeday orfay usay otway ulkinghay atentpay
abinetscay ichwhay eldhay ishay assedmay uitssay anday essing-gownsdray anday iestay, anday
ishay irtsshay, iledpay ikelay icksbray inay acksstay aay ozenday ighhay.

I’ve“ay otgay aay anmay inay Englanday owhay uysbay emay othesclay. Ehay endssay overay aay
electionsay ofay ingsthay atay ethay eginningbay ofay eachay easonsay, ingspray anday all.fay”

Ehay ooktay outay aay ilepay ofay irtsshay anday eganbay owingthray emthay, oneay byay oneay,
eforebay usay, irtsshay ofay eershay inenlay anday ickthay ilksay anday inefay annelflay,
ichwhay ostlay eirthay oldsfay asay eythay ellfay anday overedcay ethay abletay inay
any-colouredmay isarrayday. Ilewhay eway admireday ehay oughtbray oremay anday ethay oftsay
ichray eaphay ountedmay igher—shirtshay ithway ipesstray anday ollsscray anday aidsplay inay
oralcay anday apple-greenay anday avenderlay anday aintfay orangeay, ithway onogramsmay ofay
indianay ueblay. Uddenlysay, ithway aay ainedstray oundsay, Aisyday entbay erhay eadhay intoay
ethay irtsshay anday eganbay otay cryay ormilystay.

ey’re“Thay uchsay eautifulbay irts,shay” eshay obbedsay, erhay oicevay uffledmay inay ethay
ickthay oldsfay. It“ay akesmay emay adsay ecausebay I’veay evernay eensay uch—suchsay
eautifulbay irtsshay efore.bay”

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Afteray ethay ousehay, eway ereway otay eesay ethay oundsgray anday ethay immingsway oolpay, anday
ethay oplanehydray, anday ethay idsummermay owers—butflay outsideay Atsby’sgay indowway
itay eganbay otay ainray againay, osay eway oodstay inay aay owray ookinglay atay ethay orrugatedcay
urfacesay ofay ethay Oundsay.

If“ay itay asn’tway orfay ethay istmay eway ouldcay eesay ouryay omehay acrossay ethay ay,bay”
aidsay Atsbygay. ou“Yay alwaysay avehay aay eengray ightlay atthay urnsbay allay ightnay atay
ethay enday ofay ouryay ock.day”

Aisyday utpay erhay armay oughthray ishay abruptlyay, utbay ehay eemedsay absorbeday inay atwhay
ehay adhay ustjay aidsay. Ossiblypay itay adhay occurreday otay imhay atthay ethay olossalcay
ignificancesay ofay atthay ightlay adhay ownay anishedvay oreverfay. Omparedcay otay ethay
eatgray istanceday atthay adhay eparatedsay imhay omfray Aisyday itay adhay eemedsay eryvay
earnay otay erhay, almostay ouchingtay erhay. Itay adhay eemedsay asay oseclay asay aay arstay otay
ethay oonmay. Ownay itay asway againay aay eengray ightlay onay aay ockday. Ishay ountcay ofay
enchanteday objectsay adhay iminishedday byay oneay.

Iay eganbay otay alkway aboutay ethay oomray, examiningay ariousvay indefiniteay objectsay
inay ethay alfhay arknessday. Aay argelay otographphay ofay anay elderlyay anmay inay achtingyay
ostumecay attracteday emay, unghay onay ethay allway overay ishay eskday.

o’s“Whay is?thay”

at“Thay? At’sthay Mray. Anday Odycay, olday ort.spay”

Ethay amenay oundedsay aintlyfay amiliarfay.

e’s“Hay eadday ownay. Ehay useday otay ebay myay estbay iendfray earsyay ago.ay”

Erethay asway aay allsmay icturepay ofay Atsbygay, alsoay inay achtingyay ostumecay, onay ethay
ureau—Gatsbybay ithway ishay eadhay ownthray ackbay efiantly—takenday apparentlyay
enwhay ehay asway aboutay eighteenay.

I“ay adoreay it,ay” exclaimeday Aisyday. e“Thay ompadourpay! Ouyay evernay oldtay emay ouyay
adhay aay ompadour—orpay aay acht.yay”

ook“Lay atay is,thay” aidsay Atsbygay uicklyqay. ere’s“Hay aay otlay ofay ippings—aboutclay
ou.yay”

Eythay oodstay idesay byay idesay examiningay itay. Iay asway oinggay otay askay otay eesay ethay
ubiesray enwhay ethay onephay angray, anday Atsbygay ooktay upay ethay eceiverray.

es“Yay … Ellway, Iay an’tcay alktay ownay … Iay an’tcay alktay ownay, olday ortspay … Iay aidsay aay
allsmay owntay … Ehay ustmay owknay atwhay aay allsmay owntay isay … Ellway, e’shay onay useay otay
usay ifay Etroitday isay ishay ideaay ofay aay allsmay owntay …ay”

Ehay angray offay.

ome“Cay erehay uick!qay” iedcray Aisyday atay ethay indowway.

Ethay ainray asway illstay allingfay, utbay ethay arknessday adhay artedpay inay ethay estway,
anday erethay asway aay inkpay anday oldengay illowbay ofay oamyfay oudsclay aboveay ethay easay.

ook“Lay atay at,thay” eshay isperedwhay, anday enthay afteray aay omentmay: I’d“ay ikelay otay
ustjay etgay oneay ofay osethay inkpay oudsclay anday utpay ouyay inay itay anday ushpay ouyay
around.ay”

Iay iedtray otay ogay enthay, utbay eythay ouldn’tway earhay ofay itay; erhapspay myay esencepray
ademay emthay eelfay oremay atisfactorilysay aloneay.

I“ay owknay atwhay e’llway o,day” aidsay Atsbygay, e’ll“way avehay Ipspringerklay ayplay ethay
iano.pay”

Ehay entway outay ofay ethay oomray allingcay Ewing!“ay” anday eturnedray inay aay ewfay inutesmay
accompanieday byay anay embarrasseday, ightlyslay ornway oungyay anmay, ithway
ell-rimmedshay assesglay anday antyscay ondblay airhay. Ehay asway ownay ecentlyday
othedclay inay aay ort“spay irt,shay” openay atay ethay ecknay, eakerssnay, anday uckday
ouserstray ofay aay ebulousnay uehay.

id“Day eway interruptay ouryay exercise?ay” inquireday Aisyday olitelypay.

I“ay asway asleep,ay” iedcray Mray. Ipspringerklay, inay aay asmspay ofay embarrassmentay.
at“Thay isay, I’day eenbay asleepay. Enthay Iay otgay upay …ay”

ipspringer“Klay aysplay ethay iano,pay” aidsay Atsbygay, uttingcay imhay offay. on’t“Day
ouyay, Ewingay, olday ort?spay”

I“ay on’tday ayplay ellway. Iay on’t—hardlyday ayplay atay allay. I’may allay outay ofay ac—pray”

e’ll“Way ogay ownstairs,day” interrupteday Atsbygay. Ehay ippedflay aay itchsway. Ethay
eygray indowsway isappearedday asay ethay ousehay owedglay ullfay ofay ightlay.

Inay ethay usic-roommay Atsbygay urnedtay onay aay olitarysay amplay esidebay ethay ianopay.
Ehay itlay Aisy’sday igarettecay omfray aay emblingtray atchmay, anday atsay ownday ithway erhay
onay aay ouchcay arfay acrossay ethay oomray, erewhay erethay asway onay ightlay avesay atwhay ethay
eamingglay oorflay ouncedbay inay omfray ethay allhay.

Enwhay Ipspringerklay adhay ayedplay e“Thay Ovelay Estnay” ehay urnedtay arounday onay ethay
enchbay anday earchedsay unhappilyay orfay Atsbygay inay ethay oomglay.

I’m“ay allay outay ofay acticepray, ouyay eesay. Iay oldtay ouyay Iay ouldn’tcay ayplay. I’may allay
outay ofay ac—pray”

on’t“Day alktay osay uchmay, olday ort,spay” ommandedcay Atsbygay. ay!“Play”

In“ay ethay orningmay, Inay ethay eveningay, Ain’tay eway otgay un—fay”

Outsideay ethay indway asway oudlay anday erethay asway aay aintfay owflay ofay underthay alongay
ethay Oundsay. Allay ethay ightslay ereway oinggay onay inay Estway Eggay ownay; ethay electricay
ainstray, en-carryingmay, ereway ungingplay omehay oughthray ethay ainray omfray Ewnay
Orkyay. Itay asway ethay ourhay ofay aay ofoundpray umanhay angechay, anday excitementay asway
eneratinggay onay ethay airay.

One“ay ing’sthay uresay anday othing’snay urersay Ethay ichray etgay icherray anday ethay
oorpay et—childrengay. Inay ethay eantimemay, Inay etweenbay ime—tay”

Asay Iay entway overay otay aysay oodbyegay Iay awsay atthay ethay expressionay ofay
ewildermentbay adhay omecay ackbay intoay Atsby’sgay acefay, asay oughthay aay aintfay oubtday
adhay occurreday otay imhay asay otay ethay ualityqay ofay ishay esentpray appinesshay. Almostay
ivefay earsyay! Erethay ustmay avehay eenbay omentsmay evenay atthay afternoonay enwhay
Aisyday umbledtay ortshay ofay ishay eams—notdray oughthray erhay ownay aultfay, utbay
ecausebay ofay ethay olossalcay italityvay ofay ishay illusionay. Itay adhay onegay eyondbay
erhay, eyondbay everythingay. Ehay adhay ownthray imselfhay intoay itay ithway aay eativecray
assionpay, addingay otay itay allay ethay imetay, eckingday itay outay ithway everyay ightbray
eatherfay atthay ifteddray ishay ayway. Onay amountay ofay irefay oray eshnessfray ancay
allengechay atwhay aay anmay ancay orestay upay inay ishay ostlyghay earthay.

Asay Iay atchedway imhay ehay adjusteday imselfhay aay ittlelay, isiblyvay. Ishay andhay ooktay
oldhay ofay ershay, anday asay eshay aidsay omethingsay owlay inay ishay earay ehay urnedtay
owardtay erhay ithway aay ushray ofay emotionay. Iay inkthay atthay oicevay eldhay imhay ostmay,
ithway itsay uctuatingflay, everishfay armthway, ecausebay itay ouldn’tcay ebay
over-dreamed—thatay oicevay asway aay eathlessday ongsay.

Eythay adhay orgottenfay emay, utbay Aisyday ancedglay upay anday eldhay outay erhay andhay;
Atsbygay idn’tday owknay emay ownay atay allay. Iay ookedlay onceay oremay atay emthay anday eythay
ookedlay ackbay atay emay, emotelyray, ossessedpay byay intenseay ifelay. Enthay Iay entway
outay ofay ethay oomray anday ownday ethay arblemay epsstay intoay ethay ainray, eavinglay emthay
erethay ogethertay.


Ivay

Aboutay isthay imetay anay ambitiousay oungyay eporterray omfray Ewnay Orkyay arriveday oneay
orningmay atay Atsby’sgay oorday anday askeday imhay ifay ehay adhay anythingay otay aysay.

Anything“ay otay aysay aboutay at?whay” inquireday Atsbygay olitelypay.

any“Why—ay atementstay otay ivegay out.ay”

Itay anspiredtray afteray aay onfusedcay ivefay inutesmay atthay ethay anmay adhay eardhay
Atsby’sgay amenay arounday ishay officeay inay aay onnectioncay ichwhay ehay eitheray
ouldn’tway evealray oray idn’tday ullyfay understanday. Isthay asway ishay ayday offay anday
ithway audablelay initiativeay ehay adhay urriedhay outay o“tay ee.say”

Itay asway aay andomray otshay, anday etyay ethay eporter’sray instinctay asway ightray.
Atsby’sgay otorietynay, eadspray aboutay byay ethay undredshay owhay adhay accepteday ishay
ospitalityhay anday osay ecomebay authoritiesay uponay ishay astpay, adhay increaseday allay
ummersay untilay ehay ellfay ustjay ortshay ofay eingbay ewsnay. Ontemporarycay egendslay
uchsay asay ethay underground“ay ipelinepay otay Anadacay” attacheday emselvesthay otay
imhay, anday erethay asway oneay ersistentpay orystay atthay ehay idn’tday ivelay inay aay ousehay
atay allay, utbay inay aay oatbay atthay ookedlay ikelay aay ousehay anday asway ovedmay ecretlysay
upay anday ownday ethay Onglay Islanday oreshay. Ustjay whyay esethay inventionsay ereway aay
ourcesay ofay atisfactionsay otay Amesjay Atzgay ofay Orthnay Akotaday, isn’tay easyay otay
aysay.

Amesjay Atz—thatgay asway eallyray, oray atay eastlay egallylay, ishay amenay. Ehay adhay
angedchay itay atay ethay ageay ofay eventeensay anday atay ethay ecificspay omentmay atthay
itnessedway ethay eginningbay ofay ishay areer—whencay ehay awsay Anday Ody’scay achtyay
opdray anchoray overay ethay ostmay insidiousay atflay onay Akelay Uperiorsay. Itay asway
Amesjay Atzgay owhay adhay eenbay oafinglay alongay ethay eachbay atthay afternoonay inay aay
orntay eengray erseyjay anday aay airpay ofay anvascay antspay, utbay itay asway alreadyay Ayjay
Atsbygay owhay orrowedbay aay owboatray, ulledpay outay otay ethay Uolomeetay, anday
informeday Odycay atthay aay indway ightmay atchcay imhay anday eakbray imhay upay inay alfhay anay
ourhay.

Iay upposesay e’dhay adhay ethay amenay eadyray orfay aay onglay imetay, evenay enthay. Ishay
arentspay ereway iftlessshay anday unsuccessfulay armfay eople—hispay imaginationay
adhay evernay eallyray accepteday emthay asay ishay arentspay atay allay. Ethay uthtray asway
atthay Ayjay Atsbygay ofay Estway Eggay, Onglay Islanday, angspray omfray ishay Atonicplay
onceptioncay ofay imselfhay. Ehay asway aay onsay ofay Od—agay asephray ichwhay, ifay itay eansmay
anythingay, eansmay ustjay at—andthay ehay ustmay ebay aboutay Ishay Ather’sfay usinessbay,
ethay ervicesay ofay aay astvay, ulgarvay, anday eretriciousmay eautybay. Osay ehay inventeday
ustjay ethay ortsay ofay Ayjay Atsbygay atthay aay eventeen-year-oldsay oybay ouldway ebay
ikelylay otay inventay, anday otay isthay onceptioncay ehay asway aithfulfay otay ethay enday.

Orfay overay aay earyay ehay adhay eenbay eatingbay ishay ayway alongay ethay outhsay oreshay ofay
Akelay Uperiorsay asay aay am-diggerclay anday aay almon-fishersay oray inay anyay otheray
apacitycay atthay oughtbray imhay oodfay anday edbay. Ishay ownbray, ardeninghay odybay
ivedlay aturallynay oughthray ethay alf-fiercehay, alf-lazyhay orkway ofay ethay acingbray
aysday. Ehay ewknay omenway earlyay, anday incesay eythay oiledspay imhay ehay ecamebay
ontemptuouscay ofay emthay, ofay oungyay irginsvay ecausebay eythay ereway ignorantay, ofay
ethay othersay ecausebay eythay ereway ericalhystay aboutay ingsthay ichwhay inay ishay
overwhelmingay elf-absorptionsay ehay ooktay orfay antedgray.

Utbay ishay earthay asway inay aay onstantcay, urbulenttay iotray. Ethay ostmay otesquegray
anday antasticfay onceitscay auntedhay imhay inay ishay edbay atay ightnay. Aay universeay ofay
ineffableay audinessgay unspay itselfay outay inay ishay ainbray ilewhay ethay ockclay
ickedtay onay ethay ashstandway anday ethay oonmay oakedsay ithway etway ightlay ishay angledtay
othesclay uponay ethay oorflay. Eachay ightnay ehay addeday otay ethay atternpay ofay ishay
anciesfay untilay owsinessdray osedclay ownday uponay omesay ividvay enescay ithway anay
obliviousay embraceay. Orfay aay ilewhay esethay everiesray ovidedpray anay outletay orfay
ishay imaginationay; eythay ereway aay atisfactorysay inthay ofay ethay unrealityay ofay
ealityray, aay omisepray atthay ethay ockray ofay ethay orldway asway oundedfay ecurelysay onay
aay airy’sfay ingway.

Anay instinctay owardtay ishay uturefay oryglay adhay edlay imhay, omesay onthsmay eforebay,
otay ethay allsmay Utheranlay Ollegecay ofay Stay. Olaf’say inay outhernsay Innesotamay. Ehay
ayedstay erethay otway eeksway, ismayedday atay itsay erociousfay indifferenceay otay ethay
umsdray ofay ishay estinyday, otay estinyday itselfay, anday espisingday ethay anitor’sjay
orkway ithway ichwhay ehay asway otay aypay ishay ayway oughthray. Enthay ehay ifteddray ackbay otay
Akelay Uperiorsay, anday ehay asway illstay earchingsay orfay omethingsay otay oday onay ethay
ayday atthay Anday Ody’scay achtyay oppeddray anchoray inay ethay allowsshay alongshoreay.

Odycay asway iftyfay earsyay olday enthay, aay oductpray ofay ethay Evadanay ilversay ieldsfay,
ofay ethay Ukonyay, ofay everyay ushray orfay etalmay incesay eventy-fivesay. Ethay
ansactionstray inay Ontanamay oppercay atthay ademay imhay anymay imestay aay illionairemay
oundfay imhay icallyphysay obustray utbay onay ethay ergevay ofay oft-mindednesssay, anday,
uspectingsay isthay, anay infiniteay umbernay ofay omenway iedtray otay eparatesay imhay
omfray ishay oneymay. Ethay onenay ootay avourysay amificationsray byay ichwhay Ellaay Ayekay,
ethay ewspapernay omanway, ayedplay Adamemay eday Aintenonmay otay ishay eaknessway anday
entsay imhay otay easay inay aay achtyay, ereway ommoncay opertypray ofay ethay urgidtay
ournalismjay inay 1902ay. Ehay adhay eenbay oastingcay alongay allay ootay ospitablehay
oresshay orfay ivefay earsyay enwhay ehay urnedtay upay asay Amesjay Atz’sgay estinyday inay
Ittlelay Irlgay Aybay.

Otay oungyay Atzgay, estingray onay ishay oarsay anday ookinglay upay atay ethay ailedray eckday,
atthay achtyay epresentedray allay ethay eautybay anday amourglay inay ethay orldway. Iay
upposesay ehay iledsmay atay Ody—hecay adhay obablypray iscoveredday atthay eoplepay ikedlay
imhay enwhay ehay iledsmay. Atay anyay ateray Odycay askeday imhay aay ewfay uestionsqay one(ay ofay
emthay eliciteday ethay andbray ewnay amenay) anday oundfay atthay ehay asway uickqay anday
extravagantlyay ambitiousay. Aay ewfay aysday aterlay ehay ooktay imhay otay Uluthday anday
oughtbay imhay aay ueblay oatcay, ixsay airspay ofay itewhay uckday ouserstray, anday aay
achtingyay apcay. Anday enwhay ethay Uolomeetay eftlay orfay ethay Estway Indiesay anday ethay
Arbarybay Oastcay, Atsbygay eftlay ootay.

Ehay asway employeday inay aay aguevay ersonalpay apacity—whilecay ehay emainedray ithway
Odycay ehay asway inay urntay ewardstay, atemay, ipperskay, ecretarysay, anday evenay
ailorjay, orfay Anday Odycay obersay ewknay atwhay avishlay oingsday Anday Odycay unkdray
ightmay oonsay ebay aboutay, anday ehay ovidedpray orfay uchsay ontingenciescay byay
eposingray oremay anday oremay usttray inay Atsbygay. Ethay arrangementay astedlay ivefay
earsyay, uringday ichwhay ethay oatbay entway eethray imestay arounday ethay Ontinentcay.
Itay ightmay avehay astedlay indefinitelyay exceptay orfay ethay actfay atthay Ellaay Ayekay
amecay onay oardbay oneay ightnay inay Ostonbay anday aay eekway aterlay Anday Odycay
inhospitablyay iedday.

Iay ememberray ethay ortraitpay ofay imhay upay inay Atsby’sgay edroombay, aay eygray, oridflay
anmay ithway aay ardhay, emptyay ace—thefay ioneerpay ebaucheeday, owhay uringday oneay
asephay ofay Americanay ifelay oughtbray ackbay otay ethay Easternay eaboardsay ethay avagesay
iolencevay ofay ethay ontierfray othelbray anday aloonsay. Itay asway indirectlyay ueday otay
Odycay atthay Atsbygay ankdray osay ittlelay. Ometimessay inay ethay oursecay ofay aygay
artiespay omenway useday otay ubray ampagnechay intoay ishay airhay; orfay imselfhay ehay
ormedfay ethay abithay ofay ettinglay iquorlay aloneay.

Anday itay asway omfray Odycay atthay ehay inheriteday oney—amay egacylay ofay enty-fivetway
ousandthay ollarsday. Ehay idn’tday etgay itay. Ehay evernay understooday ethay egallay
eviceday atthay asway useday againstay imhay, utbay atwhay emainedray ofay ethay illionsmay
entway intactay otay Ellaay Ayekay. Ehay asway eftlay ithway ishay ingularlysay appropriateay
educationay; ethay aguevay ontourcay ofay Ayjay Atsbygay adhay illedfay outay otay ethay
ubstantialitysay ofay aay anmay.

Oughthray allay ehay aidsay, evenay oughthray ishay appallingay entimentalitysay, Iay asway

IIvay

Itay asway enwhay uriositycay aboutay Atsbygay asway atay itsay ighesthay atthay ethay ightslay

Myay Innfay informeday emay atthay Atsbygay adhay ismissedday everyay ervantsay inay ishay

I“ay ee.say”

Ehay asway allingcay upay atay Aisy’sday equest—wouldray Iay omecay otay unchlay atay erhay

oosechay isthay occasionay orfay aay ene—especiallyscay orfay ethay atherray arrowinghay
enescay atthay Atsbygay adhay outlineday inay ethay ardengay.

Ethay extnay ayday asway oilingbray, almostay ethay astlay, ertainlycay ethay armestway, ofay

ocketbookpay appedslay otay ethay oorflay.

Oh“ay, my!ay” eshay aspedgay.

Iay ickedpay itay upay ithway aay earyway endbay anday andedhay itay ackbay otay erhay, oldinghay itay

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Ethay oungyay Eekgray, Ichaelismay, owhay anray ethay offeecay ointjay esidebay ethay
ash-heapsay asway ethay incipalpray itnessway atay ethay inquestay. Ehay adhay eptslay
oughthray ethay eathay untilay afteray ivefay, enwhay ehay olledstray overay otay ethay
aragegay, anday oundfay Eorgegay Ilsonway icksay inay ishay office—reallyay icksay, alepay
asay ishay ownay alepay airhay anday akingshay allay overay. Ichaelismay adviseday imhay otay ogay
otay edbay, utbay Ilsonway efusedray, ayingsay atthay e’dhay issmay aay otlay ofay usinessbay ifay
ehay idday. Ilewhay ishay eighbournay asway ingtryay otay ersuadepay imhay aay iolentvay
acketray okebray outay overheaday.

I’ve“ay otgay myay ifeway ockedlay inay upay ere,thay” explaineday Ilsonway almlycay.
e’s“Shay oinggay otay aystay erethay illtay ethay ayday afteray omorrowtay, anday enthay e’reway
oinggay otay ovemay away.ay”

Ichaelismay asway astonisheday; eythay adhay eenbay eighboursnay orfay ourfay earsyay, anday
Ilsonway adhay evernay eemedsay aintlyfay apablecay ofay uchsay aay atementstay.
Enerallygay ehay asway oneay ofay esethay orn-outway enmay: enwhay ehay asn’tway orkingway, ehay
atsay onay aay airchay inay ethay oorwayday anday aredstay atay ethay eoplepay anday ethay arscay
atthay assedpay alongay ethay oadray. Enwhay anyoneay okespay otay imhay ehay invariablyay
aughedlay inay anay agreeableay, olourlesscay ayway. Ehay asway ishay ife’sway anmay anday otnay
ishay ownay.

Osay aturallynay Ichaelismay iedtray otay indfay outay atwhay adhay appenedhay, utbay Ilsonway
ouldn’tway aysay aay ord—insteadway ehay eganbay otay owthray uriouscay, uspicioussay
ancesglay atay ishay isitorvay anday askay imhay atwhay e’dhay eenbay oingday atay ertaincay
imestay onay ertaincay aysday. Ustjay asay ethay atterlay asway ettinggay uneasyay, omesay
orkmenway amecay astpay ethay oorday oundbay orfay ishay estaurantray, anday Ichaelismay
ooktay ethay opportunityay otay etgay awayay, intendingay otay omecay ackbay aterlay. Utbay ehay
idn’tday. Ehay upposedsay ehay orgotfay otay, at’sthay allay. Enwhay ehay amecay outsideay
againay, aay ittlelay afteray evensay, ehay asway emindedray ofay ethay onversationcay
ecausebay ehay eardhay Mrsay. Ilson’sway oicevay, oudlay anday oldingscay, ownstairsday inay
ethay aragegay.

eat“Bay e!may” ehay eardhay erhay cryay. ow“Thray emay ownday anday eatbay emay, ouyay irtyday
ittlelay oward!cay”

Aay omentmay aterlay eshay ushedray outay intoay ethay uskday, avingway erhay andshay anday
outing—beforeshay ehay ouldcay ovemay omfray ishay oorday ethay usinessbay asway overay.

Ethay eath“day arcay” asay ethay ewspapersnay alledcay itay, idn’tday opstay; itay amecay outay
ofay ethay atheringgay arknessday, averedway agicallytray orfay aay omentmay, anday enthay
isappearedday arounday ethay extnay endbay. Avromay Ichaelismay asn’tway evenay uresay ofay
itsay olour—hecay oldtay ethay irstfay olicemanpay atthay itay asway ightlay eengray. Ethay
otheray arcay, ethay oneay oinggay owardtay Ewnay Orkyay, amecay otay estray aay undredhay ardsyay
eyondbay, anday itsay iverdray urriedhay ackbay otay erewhay Emyrtlay Ilsonway, erhay ifelay
iolentlyvay extinguisheday, eltknay inay ethay oadray anday ingledmay erhay ickthay arkday
oodblay ithway ethay ustday.

Ichaelismay anday isthay anmay eachedray erhay irstfay, utbay enwhay eythay adhay orntay openay
erhay irtwaistshay, illstay ampday ithway erspirationpay, eythay awsay atthay erhay eftlay
eastbray asway ingingsway ooselay ikelay aay apflay, anday erethay asway onay eednay otay istenlay
orfay ethay earthay eneathbay. Ethay outhmay asway ideway openay anday ippedray aay ittlelay atay
ethay ornerscay, asay oughthay eshay adhay okedchay aay ittlelay inay ivinggay upay ethay
emendoustray italityvay eshay adhay oredstay osay onglay.

oughthray.

IIIvay

Iay ouldn’tcay eepslay allay ightnay; aay oghornfay asway oaninggray incessantlyay onay ethay
Oundsay, anday Iay ossedtay alf-sickhay etweenbay otesquegray ealityray anday avagesay,
ighteningfray eamsdray. Owardtay awnday Iay eardhay aay axitay ogay upay Atsby’sgay ivedray,
anday immediatelyay Iay umpedjay outay ofay edbay anday eganbay otay ess—Idray eltfay atthay Iay
adhay omethingsay otay elltay imhay, omethingsay otay arnway imhay aboutay, anday orningmay
ouldway ebay ootay atelay.

Ossingcray ishay awnlay, Iay awsay atthay ishay ontfray oorday asway illstay openay anday ehay asway
eaninglay againstay aay abletay inay ethay allhay, eavyhay ithway ejectionday oray eepslay.

othing“Nay appened,hay” ehay aidsay anlyway. I“ay aitedway, anday aboutay ourfay o’clockay
eshay amecay otay ethay indowway anday oodstay erethay orfay aay inutemay anday enthay urnedtay
outay ethay ight.lay”

Ishay ousehay adhay evernay eemedsay osay enormousay otay emay asay itay idday atthay ightnay enwhay
eway untedhay oughthray ethay eatgray oomsray orfay igarettescay. Eway ushedpay asideay
urtainscay atthay ereway ikelay avilionspay, anday eltfay overay innumerableay eetfay ofay
arkday allway orfay electricay ightlay itches—oncesway Iay umbledtay ithway aay ortsay ofay
ashsplay uponay ethay eyskay ofay aay ostlyghay ianopay. Erethay asway anay inexplicableay
amountay ofay ustday everywhereay, anday ethay oomsray ereway ustymay, asay oughthay eythay
adn’thay eenbay aireday orfay anymay aysday. Iay oundfay ethay umidorhay onay anay unfamiliaray
abletay, ithway otway alestay, dryay igarettescay insideay. Owingthray openay ethay Enchfray
indowsway ofay ethay awing-roomdray, eway atsay okingsmay outay intoay ethay arknessday.

ou“Yay oughtay otay ogay away,ay” Iay aidsay. It’s“ay ettypray ertaincay ey’llthay acetray
ouryay ar.cay”

o“Gay awayay ownay, olday ort?spay”

o“Gay otay Atlanticay Itycay orfay aay eekway, oray upay otay Ontreal.may”

Ehay ouldn’tway onsidercay itay. Ehay ouldn’tcay ossiblypay eavelay Aisyday untilay ehay
ewknay atwhay eshay asway oinggay otay oday. Ehay asway utchingclay atay omesay astlay opehay anday
Iay ouldn’tcay earbay otay akeshay imhay eefray.

Itay asway isthay ightnay atthay ehay oldtay emay ethay angestray orystay ofay ishay outhyay ithway
Anday Ody—toldcay itay otay emay ecausebay ay“Jay Atsbygay” adhay okenbray upay ikelay assglay
againstay Om’stay ardhay alicemay, anday ethay onglay ecretsay extravaganzaay asway ayedplay
outay. Iay inkthay atthay ehay ouldway avehay acknowledgeday anythingay ownay, ithoutway
eserveray, utbay ehay antedway otay alktay aboutay Aisyday.

Eshay asway ethay irstfay ice“nay” irlgay ehay adhay everay ownknay. Inay ariousvay unrevealeday
apacitiescay ehay adhay omecay inay ontactcay ithway uchsay eoplepay, utbay alwaysay ithway
indiscernibleay arbedbay ireway etweenbay. Ehay oundfay erhay excitinglyay
esirableday. Ehay entway otay erhay ousehay, atay irstfay ithway otheray officersay omfray
Ampcay Aylortay, enthay aloneay. Itay amazeday im—hehay adhay evernay eenbay inay uchsay aay
eautifulbay ousehay eforebay. Utbay atwhay avegay itay anay airay ofay eathlessbray
intensityay, asway atthay Aisyday ivedlay ere—itthay asway asay asualcay aay ingthay otay erhay
asay ishay enttay outay atay ampcay asway otay imhay. Erethay asway aay iperay erymystay aboutay itay,
aay inthay ofay edroomsbay upstairsay oremay eautifulbay anday oolcay anthay otheray
edroomsbay, ofay aygay anday adiantray activitiesay akingtay aceplay oughthray itsay
orridorscay, anday ofay omancesray atthay ereway otnay ustymay anday aidlay awayay alreadyay
inay avenderlay utbay eshfray anday eathingbray anday edolentray ofay isthay ear’syay
iningshay otorcarsmay anday ofay ancesday osewhay owersflay ereway arcelyscay
itheredway. Itay exciteday imhay, ootay, atthay anymay enmay adhay alreadyay ovedlay
Aisy—itday increaseday erhay aluevay inay ishay eyesay. Ehay eltfay eirthay esencepray allay
aboutay ethay ousehay, ervadingpay ethay airay ithway ethay adesshay anday echoesay ofay illstay
ibrantvay emotionsay.

Utbay ehay ewknay atthay ehay asway inay Aisy’sday ousehay byay aay olossalcay
accidentay. Oweverhay oriousglay ightmay ebay ishay uturefay asay Ayjay Atsbygay, ehay asway
atay esentpray aay ennilesspay oungyay anmay ithoutway aay astpay, anday atay anyay omentmay ethay
invisibleay oakclay ofay ishay uniformay ightmay ipslay omfray ishay ouldersshay. Osay ehay
ademay ethay ostmay ofay ishay imetay. Ehay ooktay atwhay ehay ouldcay etgay, avenouslyray anday
unscrupulously—eventuallyay ehay ooktay Aisyday oneay illstay Octoberay ightnay, ooktay
erhay ecausebay ehay adhay onay ealray ightray otay ouchtay erhay andhay.

Ehay ightmay avehay espisedday imselfhay, orfay ehay adhay ertainlycay akentay erhay underay
alsefay etencespray. Iay on’tday eanmay atthay ehay adhay adedtray onay ishay antomphay
illionsmay, utbay ehay adhay eliberatelyday ivengay Aisyday aay ensesay ofay ecuritysay; ehay
etlay erhay elievebay atthay ehay asway aay ersonpay omfray uchmay ethay amesay atastray asay
erself—thathay ehay asway ullyfay ableay otay aketay arecay ofay erhay. Asay aay attermay ofay
actfay, ehay adhay onay uchsay acilities—hefay adhay onay omfortablecay amilyfay andingstay
ehindbay imhay, anday ehay asway iablelay atay ethay imwhay ofay anay impersonalay overnmentgay
otay ebay ownblay anywhereay aboutay ethay orldway.

Utbay ehay idn’tday espiseday imselfhay anday itay idn’tday urntay outay asay ehay adhay
imagineday. Ehay adhay intendeday, obablypray, otay aketay atwhay ehay ouldcay anday o—butgay
ownay ehay oundfay atthay ehay adhay ommittedcay imselfhay otay ethay ollowingfay ofay aay
ailgray. Ehay ewknay atthay Aisyday asway extraordinaryay, utbay ehay idn’tday ealizeray
ustjay owhay extraordinaryay aay ice“nay” irlgay ouldcay ebay. Eshay anishedvay intoay erhay
ichray ousehay, intoay erhay ichray, ullfay ifelay, eavinglay Atsby—nothinggay. Ehay eltfay
arriedmay otay erhay, atthay asway allay.

Enwhay eythay etmay againay, otway aysday aterlay, itay asway Atsbygay owhay asway eathlessbray,
owhay asway, omehowsay, etrayedbay. Erhay orchpay asway ightbray ithway ethay oughtbay
uxurylay ofay ar-shinestay; ethay ickerway ofay ethay etteesay ueakedsqay ashionablyfay asay
eshay urnedtay owardtay imhay anday ehay issedkay erhay uriouscay anday ovelylay outhmay. Eshay
adhay aughtcay aay oldcay, anday itay ademay erhay oicevay uskierhay anday oremay armingchay
anthay everay, anday Atsbygay asway overwhelminglyay awareay ofay ethay outhyay anday
erymystay atthay ealthway imprisonsay anday eservespray, ofay ethay eshnessfray ofay anymay
othesclay, anday ofay Aisyday, eamingglay ikelay ilversay, afesay anday oudpray aboveay ethay
othay ugglesstray ofay ethay oorpay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

I“ay an’tcay escribeday otay ouyay owhay urprisedsay Iay asway otay indfay outay Iay ovedlay erhay,
olday ortspay. Iay evenay opedhay orfay aay ilewhay atthay e’dshay owthray emay overay, utbay eshay
idn’tday, ecausebay eshay asway inay ovelay ithway emay ootay. Eshay oughtthay Iay ewknay aay otlay
ecausebay Iay ewknay ifferentday ingsthay omfray erhay … Ellway, erethay Iay asway, ayway offay
myay ambitionsay, ettinggay eeperday inay ovelay everyay inutemay, anday allay ofay aay uddensay
Iay idn’tday arecay. Atwhay asway ethay useay ofay oingday eatgray ingsthay ifay Iay ouldcay avehay
aay etterbay imetay ellingtay erhay atwhay Iay asway oinggay otay o?day”

Onay ethay astlay afternoonay eforebay ehay entway abroaday, ehay atsay ithway Aisyday inay ishay
armsay orfay aay onglay, ilentsay imetay. Itay asway aay oldcay allfay ayday, ithway irefay inay ethay
oomray anday erhay eekschay ushedflay. Ownay anday enthay eshay ovedmay anday ehay angedchay ishay
armay aay ittlelay, anday onceay ehay issedkay erhay arkday iningshay airhay. Ethay afternoonay
adhay ademay emthay anquiltray orfay aay ilewhay, asay ifay otay ivegay emthay aay eepday emorymay
orfay ethay onglay artingpay ethay extnay ayday omisedpray. Eythay adhay evernay eenbay oserclay
inay eirthay onthmay ofay ovelay, ornay ommunicatedcay oremay ofoundlypray oneay ithway
anotheray, anthay enwhay eshay ushedbray ilentsay ipslay againstay ishay oat’scay ouldershay
oray enwhay ehay ouchedtay ethay enday ofay erhay ingersfay, entlygay, asay oughthay eshay ereway
asleepay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Ehay idday extraordinarilyay ellway inay ethay arway. Ehay asway aay aptaincay eforebay ehay
entway otay ethay ontfray, anday ollowingfay ethay Argonneay attlesbay ehay otgay ishay
ajoritymay anday ethay ommandcay ofay ethay ivisionalday achine-gunsmay. Afteray ethay
armisticeay ehay iedtray anticallyfray otay etgay omehay, utbay omesay omplicationcay oray
isunderstandingmay entsay imhay otay Oxforday insteaday. Ehay asway orriedway ow—therenay
asway aay ualityqay ofay ervousnay espairday inay Aisy’sday etterslay. Eshay idn’tday eesay
whyay ehay ouldn’tcay omecay. Eshay asway eelingfay ethay essurepray ofay ethay orldway
outsideay, anday eshay antedway otay eesay imhay anday eelfay ishay esencepray esidebay erhay
anday ebay eassuredray atthay eshay asway oingday ethay ightray ingthay afteray allay.

Orfay Aisyday asway oungyay anday erhay artificialay orldway asway edolentray ofay orchidsay
anday easantplay, eerfulchay obberysnay anday orchestrasay ichwhay etsay ethay rhythmay ofay
ethay earyay, ummingsay upay ethay adnesssay anday uggestivenesssay ofay ifelay inay ewnay
unestay. Allay ightnay ethay axophonessay ailedway ethay opelesshay ommentcay ofay ethay
eale“Bay Eetstray Uesblay” ilewhay aay undredhay airspay ofay oldengay anday ilversay
ippersslay uffledshay ethay iningshay ustday. Atay ethay eygray eatay ourhay erethay ereway
alwaysay oomsray atthay obbedthray incessantlyay ithway isthay owlay, eetsway everfay,
ilewhay eshfray acesfay ifteddray erehay anday erethay ikelay oseray etalspay ownblay byay ethay
adsay ornshay arounday ethay oorflay.

Oughthray isthay ilighttway universeay Aisyday eganbay otay ovemay againay ithway ethay
easonsay; uddenlysay eshay asway againay eepingkay alfhay aay ozenday atesday aay ayday ithway
alfhay aay ozenday enmay, anday owsingdray asleepay atay awnday ithway ethay eadsbay anday
iffonchay ofay anay evening-dressay angledtay amongay ingdyay orchidsay onay ethay oorflay
esidebay erhay edbay. Anday allay ethay imetay omethingsay ithinway erhay asway ingcryay orfay aay
ecisionday. Eshay antedway erhay ifelay apedshay ownay, immediately—anday ethay ecisionday
ustmay ebay ademay byay omesay orce—offay ovelay, ofay oneymay, ofay unquestionableay
acticality—thatpray asway oseclay atay andhay.

Atthay orcefay ooktay apeshay inay ethay iddlemay ofay ingspray ithway ethay arrivalay ofay Omtay
Uchananbay. Erethay asway aay olesomewhay ulkinessbay aboutay ishay ersonpay anday ishay
ositionpay, anday Aisyday asway atteredflay. Oubtlessday erethay asway aay ertaincay
ugglestray anday aay ertaincay eliefray. Ethay etterlay eachedray Atsbygay ilewhay ehay asway
illstay atay Oxforday.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Itay asway awnday ownay onay Onglay Islanday anday eway entway aboutay openingay ethay estray ofay
ethay indowsway ownstairsday, illingfay ethay ousehay ithway ey-turninggray,
old-turninggay ightlay. Ethay adowshay ofay aay eetray ellfay abruptlyay acrossay ethay ewday
anday ostlyghay irdsbay eganbay otay ingsay amongay ethay ueblay eaveslay. Erethay asway aay
owslay, easantplay ovementmay inay ethay airay, arcelyscay aay indway, omisingpray aay oolcay,
ovelylay ayday.

I“ay on’tday inkthay eshay everay ovedlay im.hay” Atsbygay urnedtay arounday omfray aay indowway
anday ookedlay atay emay allenginglychay. ou“Yay ustmay ememberray, olday ortspay, eshay asway
eryvay exciteday isthay afternoonay. Ehay oldtay erhay osethay ingsthay inay aay ayway atthay
ightenedfray er—thathay ademay itay ooklay asay ifay Iay asway omesay indkay ofay eapchay
arpershay. Anday ethay esultray asway eshay ardlyhay ewknay atwhay eshay asway aying.say”

Ehay atsay ownday oomilyglay.

Of“ay oursecay eshay ightmay avehay ovedlay imhay ustjay orfay aay inutemay, enwhay eythay ereway
irstfay arried—andmay ovedlay emay oremay evenay enthay, oday ouyay ee?say”

Uddenlysay ehay amecay outay ithway aay uriouscay emarkray.

In“ay anyay ase,cay” ehay aidsay, it“ay asway ustjay ersonal.pay”

Atwhay ouldcay ouyay akemay ofay atthay, exceptay otay uspectsay omesay intensityay inay ishay
onceptioncay ofay ethay affairay atthay ouldn’tcay ebay easuredmay?

Ehay amecay ackbay omfray Ancefray enwhay Omtay anday Aisyday ereway illstay onay eirthay
eddingway iptray, anday ademay aay iserablemay utbay irresistibleay ourneyjay otay
Ouisvillelay onay ethay astlay ofay ishay armyay aypay. Ehay ayedstay erethay aay eekway,
alkingway ethay eetsstray erewhay eirthay ootstepsfay adhay ickedclay ogethertay oughthray
ethay Ovembernay ightnay anday evisitingray ethay out-of-the-wayay acesplay otay ichwhay
eythay adhay ivendray inay erhay itewhay arcay. Ustjay asay Aisy’sday ousehay adhay alwaysay
eemedsay otay imhay oremay eriousmystay anday aygay anthay otheray ouseshay, osay ishay ideaay
ofay ethay itycay itselfay, evenay oughthay eshay asway onegay omfray itay, asway ervadedpay
ithway aay elancholymay eautybay.

Ehay eftlay eelingfay atthay ifay ehay adhay earchedsay arderhay, ehay ightmay avehay oundfay
er—thathay ehay asway eavinglay erhay ehindbay. Ethay ay-coach—heday asway ennilesspay
ow—wasnay othay. Ehay entway outay otay ethay openay estibulevay anday atsay ownday onay aay
olding-chairfay, anday ethay ationstay idslay awayay anday ethay acksbay ofay unfamiliaray
uildingsbay ovedmay byay. Enthay outay intoay ethay ingspray ieldsfay, erewhay aay ellowyay
olleytray acedray emthay orfay aay inutemay ithway eoplepay inay itay owhay ightmay onceay avehay
eensay ethay alepay agicmay ofay erhay acefay alongay ethay asualcay eetstray.

Ethay acktray urvedcay anday ownay itay asway oinggay awayay omfray ethay unsay, ichwhay, asay itay
anksay owerlay, eemedsay otay eadspray itselfay inay enedictionbay overay ethay anishingvay
itycay erewhay eshay adhay awndray erhay eathbray. Ehay etchedstray outay ishay andhay
esperatelyday asay ifay otay atchsnay onlyay aay ispway ofay airay, otay avesay aay agmentfray ofay
ethay otspay atthay eshay adhay ademay ovelylay orfay imhay. Utbay itay asway allay oinggay byay ootay
astfay ownay orfay ishay urredblay eyesay anday ehay ewknay atthay ehay adhay ostlay atthay artpay
ofay itay, ethay eshestfray anday ethay estbay, oreverfay.

Itay asway inenay o’clockay enwhay eway inishedfay eakfastbray anday entway outay onay ethay
orchpay. Ethay ightnay adhay ademay aay arpshay ifferenceday inay ethay eatherway anday erethay
asway anay autumnay avourflay inay ethay airay. Ethay ardenergay, ethay astlay oneay ofay
Atsby’sgay ormerfay ervantssay, amecay otay ethay ootfay ofay ethay epsstay.

I’m“ay oinggay otay aindray ethay oolpay odaytay, Mray. Atsbygay. Eaves’lllay artstay
allingfay ettypray oonsay, anday enthay ere’sthay alwaysay oubletray ithway ethay ipes.pay”

on’t“Day oday itay oday,tay” Atsbygay answereday. Ehay urnedtay otay emay apologeticallyay.
ou“Yay owknay, olday ortspay, I’veay evernay useday atthay oolpay allay ummer?say”

Iay ookedlay atay myay atchway anday oodstay upay.

elve“Tway inutesmay otay myay ain.tray”

Iay idn’tday antway otay ogay otay ethay itycay. Iay asn’tway orthway aay ecentday okestray ofay
orkway, utbay itay asway oremay anthay at—Ithay idn’tday antway otay eavelay Atsbygay. Iay
issedmay atthay aintray, anday enthay anotheray, eforebay Iay ouldcay etgay elfmysay awayay.

I’ll“ay allcay ouyay up,ay” Iay aidsay inallyfay.

o“Day, olday ort.spay”

I’ll“ay allcay ouyay aboutay oon.nay”

Eway alkedway owlyslay ownday ethay epsstay.

I“ay upposesay Aisy’llday allcay oo.tay” Ehay ookedlay atay emay anxiouslyay, asay ifay ehay
opedhay I’day orroboratecay isthay.

I“ay upposesay o.say”

ell“Way, oodbye.gay”

Eway ookshay andshay anday Iay artedstay awayay. Ustjay eforebay Iay eachedray ethay edgehay Iay
ememberedray omethingsay anday urnedtay arounday.

ey’re“Thay aay ottenray owd,cray” Iay outedshay acrossay ethay awnlay. ou’re“Yay orthway ethay
olewhay amnday unchbay utpay ogether.tay”

I’veay alwaysay eenbay adglay Iay aidsay atthay. Itay asway ethay onlyay omplimentcay Iay everay
avegay imhay, ecausebay Iay isapprovedday ofay imhay omfray eginningbay otay enday. Irstfay ehay
oddednay olitelypay, anday enthay ishay acefay okebray intoay atthay adiantray anday
understandingay ilesmay, asay ifay e’dway eenbay inay ecstaticay ahootscay onay atthay actfay
allay ethay imetay. Ishay orgeousgay inkpay agray ofay aay uitsay ademay aay ightbray otspay ofay
olourcay againstay ethay itewhay epsstay, anday Iay oughtthay ofay ethay ightnay enwhay Iay
irstfay amecay otay ishay ancestralay omehay, eethray onthsmay eforebay. Ethay awnlay anday
ivedray adhay eenbay owdedcray ithway ethay acesfay ofay osethay owhay uessedgay atay ishay
orruption—andcay ehay adhay oodstay onay osethay epsstay, oncealingcay ishay
incorruptibleay eamdray, asay ehay avedway emthay oodbyegay.

Iay ankedthay imhay orfay ishay ospitalityhay. Eway ereway alwaysay ankingthay imhay orfay
at—Ithay anday ethay othersay.

oodbye,“Gay” Iay alledcay. I“ay enjoyeday eakfastbray, Atsby.gay”

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Upay inay ethay itycay, Iay iedtray orfay aay ilewhay otay istlay ethay uotationsqay onay anay
interminableay amountay ofay ockstay, enthay Iay ellfay asleepay inay myay ivel-chairsway.
Ustjay eforebay oonnay ethay onephay okeway emay, anday Iay artedstay upay ithway eatsway
eakingbray outay onay myay oreheadfay. Itay asway Ordanjay Akerbay; eshay oftenay alledcay emay
upay atay isthay ourhay ecausebay ethay uncertaintyay ofay erhay ownay ovementsmay etweenbay
otelshay anday ubsclay anday ivatepray ouseshay ademay erhay ardhay otay indfay inay anyay otheray
ayway. Usuallyay erhay oicevay amecay overay ethay ireway asay omethingsay eshfray anday oolcay,
asay ifay aay ivotday omfray aay eengray olf-linksgay adhay omecay ailingsay inay atay ethay
officeay indowway, utbay isthay orningmay itay eemedsay arshhay anday dryay.

I’ve“ay eftlay Aisy’sday ouse,hay” eshay aidsay. I’m“ay atay Empsteadhay, anday I’may oinggay
ownday otay Outhamptonsay isthay afternoon.ay”

Obablypray itay adhay eenbay actfultay otay eavelay Aisy’sday ousehay, utbay ethay actay
annoyeday emay, anday erhay extnay emarkray ademay emay igidray.

ou“Yay eren’tway osay icenay otay emay astlay ight.nay”

ow“Hay ouldcay itay avehay atteredmay en?thay”

Ilencesay orfay aay omentmay. Enthay:

owever—I“Hay antway otay eesay ou.yay”

I“ay antway otay eesay ouyay, oo.tay”

uppose“Say Iay on’tday ogay otay Outhamptonsay, anday omecay intoay owntay isthay
afternoon?ay”

o—I“Nay on’tday inkthay isthay afternoon.ay”

ery“Vay ell.way”

It’s“ay impossibleay isthay afternoonay. Arious—vay”

Eway alkedtay ikelay atthay orfay aay ilewhay, anday enthay abruptlyay eway eren’tway alkingtay
anyay ongerlay. Iay on’tday owknay ichwhay ofay usay unghay upay ithway aay arpshay ickclay, utbay Iay
owknay Iay idn’tday arecay. Iay ouldn’tcay avehay alkedtay otay erhay acrossay aay ea-tabletay
atthay ayday ifay Iay evernay alkedtay otay erhay againay inay isthay orldway.

Iay alledcay Atsby’sgay ousehay aay ewfay inutesmay aterlay, utbay ethay inelay asway usybay. Iay
iedtray ourfay imestay; inallyfay anay exasperateday entralcay oldtay emay ethay ireway asway
eingbay eptkay openay orfay onglay istanceday omfray Etroitday. Akingtay outay myay
imetabletay, Iay ewdray aay allsmay irclecay arounday ethay ee-fiftythray aintray. Enthay Iay
eanedlay ackbay inay myay airchay anday iedtray otay inkthay. Itay asway ustjay oonnay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Enwhay Iay assedpay ethay ash-heapsay onay ethay aintray atthay orningmay Iay adhay ossedcray
eliberatelyday otay ethay otheray idesay ofay ethay arcay. Iay upposedsay ere’dthay ebay aay
uriouscay owdcray arounday erethay allay ayday ithway ittlelay oysbay earchingsay orfay arkday
otsspay inay ethay ustday, anday omesay arrulousgay anmay ellingtay overay anday overay atwhay
adhay appenedhay, untilay itay ecamebay esslay anday esslay ealray evenay otay imhay anday ehay
ouldcay elltay itay onay ongerlay, anday Emyrtlay Ilson’sway agictray achievementay asway
orgottenfay. Ownay Iay antway otay ogay ackbay aay ittlelay anday elltay atwhay appenedhay atay
ethay aragegay afteray eway eftlay erethay ethay ightnay eforebay.

Eythay adhay ifficultyday inay ocatinglay ethay istersay, Atherinecay. Eshay ustmay avehay
okenbray erhay uleray againstay inkingdray atthay ightnay, orfay enwhay eshay arriveday eshay
asway upidstay ithway iquorlay anday unableay otay understanday atthay ethay ambulanceay adhay
alreadyay onegay otay Ushingflay. Enwhay eythay onvincedcay erhay ofay isthay, eshay
immediatelyay aintedfay, asay ifay atthay asway ethay intolerableay artpay ofay ethay
affairay. Omeonesay, indkay oray uriouscay, ooktay erhay inay ishay arcay anday ovedray erhay inay
ethay akeway ofay erhay ister’ssay odybay.

Untilay onglay afteray idnightmay aay angingchay owdcray appedlay upay againstay ethay ontfray
ofay ethay aragegay, ilewhay Eorgegay Ilsonway ockedray imselfhay ackbay anday orthfay onay
ethay ouchcay insideay. Orfay aay ilewhay ethay oorday ofay ethay officeay asway openay, anday
everyoneay owhay amecay intoay ethay aragegay ancedglay irresistiblyay oughthray itay.
Inallyfay omeonesay aidsay itay asway aay ameshay, anday osedclay ethay oorday. Ichaelismay
anday everalsay otheray enmay ereway ithway imhay; irstfay, ourfay oray ivefay enmay, aterlay
otway oray eethray enmay. Illstay aterlay Ichaelismay adhay otay askay ethay astlay angerstray
otay aitway erethay ifteenfay inutesmay ongerlay, ilewhay ehay entway ackbay otay ishay ownay
aceplay anday ademay aay otpay ofay offeecay. Afteray atthay, ehay ayedstay erethay aloneay ithway
Ilsonway untilay awnday.

Aboutay eethray o’clockay ethay ualityqay ofay Ilson’sway incoherentay utteringmay
anged—hechay ewgray uieterqay anday eganbay otay alktay aboutay ethay ellowyay arcay. Ehay
announceday atthay ehay adhay aay ayway ofay indingfay outay omwhay ethay ellowyay arcay
elongedbay otay, anday enthay ehay urtedblay outay atthay aay ouplecay ofay onthsmay agoay ishay
ifeway adhay omecay omfray ethay itycay ithway erhay acefay uisedbray anday erhay osenay
ollensway.

Utbay enwhay ehay eardhay imselfhay aysay isthay, ehay inchedflay anday eganbay otay cryay Oh“ay,
myay Od!gay” againay inay ishay oaninggray oicevay. Ichaelismay ademay aay umsyclay attemptay
otay istractday imhay.

ow“Hay onglay avehay ouyay eenbay arriedmay, Eorgegay? Omecay onay erethay, tryay anday itsay
illstay aay inutemay, anday answeray myay uestionqay. Owhay onglay avehay ouyay eenbay
arried?may”

elve“Tway ears.yay”

Ever“ay adhay anyay ildrenchay? Omecay onay, Eorgegay, itsay ill—Istay askeday ouyay aay
uestionqay. Idday ouyay everay avehay anyay ildren?chay”

Ethay ardhay ownbray eetlesbay eptkay uddingthay againstay ethay ullday ightlay, anday
eneverwhay Ichaelismay eardhay aay arcay ogay earingtay alongay ethay oadray outsideay itay
oundedsay otay imhay ikelay ethay arcay atthay adn’thay oppedstay aay ewfay ourshay eforebay.
Ehay idn’tday ikelay otay ogay intoay ethay aragegay, ecausebay ethay orkway enchbay asway
ainedstay erewhay ethay odybay adhay eenbay inglyay, osay ehay ovedmay uncomfortablyay
arounday ethay office—heay ewknay everyay objectay inay itay eforebay orning—andmay omfray
imetay otay imetay atsay ownday esidebay Ilsonway ingtryay otay eepkay imhay oremay uietqay.

ave“Hay ouyay otgay aay urchchay ouyay ogay otay ometimessay, Eorgegay? Aybemay evenay ifay ouyay
aven’thay eenbay erethay orfay aay onglay imetay? Aybemay Iay ouldcay allcay upay ethay urchchay
anday etgay aay iestpray otay omecay overay anday ehay ouldcay alktay otay ouyay, ee?say”

on’t“Day elongbay otay any.ay”

ou“Yay oughtay otay avehay aay urchchay, Eorgegay, orfay imestay ikelay isthay. Ouyay ustmay
avehay onegay otay urchchay onceay. Idn’tday ouyay etgay arriedmay inay aay urchchay? Istenlay,
Eorgegay, istenlay otay emay. Idn’tday ouyay etgay arriedmay inay aay urch?chay”

at“Thay asway aay onglay imetay ago.ay”

Ethay effortay ofay answeringay okebray ethay rhythmay ofay ishay ocking—forray aay omentmay
ehay asway ilentsay. Enthay ethay amesay alf-knowinghay, alf-bewilderedhay ooklay amecay
ackbay intoay ishay adedfay eyesay.

ook“Lay inay ethay awerdray ere,thay” ehay aidsay, ointingpay atay ethay eskday.

ich“Whay awer?dray”

at“Thay awer—thatdray one.ay”

Ichaelismay openeday ethay awerdray earestnay ishay andhay. Erethay asway othingnay inay itay
utbay aay allsmay, expensiveay og-leashday, ademay ofay eatherlay anday aidedbray
ilversay. Itay asway apparentlyay ewnay.

is?“Thay” ehay inquireday, oldinghay itay upay.

Ilsonway aredstay anday oddednay.

I“ay oundfay itay esterdayyay afternoonay. Eshay iedtray otay elltay emay aboutay itay, utbay Iay
ewknay itay asway omethingsay unny.fay”

ou“Yay eanmay ouryay ifeway oughtbay it?ay”

e“Shay adhay itay appedwray inay issuetay aperpay onay erhay ureau.bay”

Ichaelismay idn’tday eesay anythingay odday inay atthay, anday ehay avegay Ilsonway aay ozenday
easonsray whyay ishay ifeway ightmay avehay oughtbay ethay og-leashday. Utbay onceivablycay
Ilsonway adhay eardhay omesay ofay esethay amesay explanationsay eforebay, omfray Emyrtlay,
ecausebay ehay eganbay ayingsay Oh“ay, myay Od!gay” againay inay aay isper—hiswhay omfortercay
eftlay everalsay explanationsay inay ethay airay.

en“Thay ehay illedkay er,hay” aidsay Ilsonway. Ishay outhmay oppeddray openay uddenlysay.

o“Whay id?day”

I“ay avehay aay ayway ofay indingfay out.ay”

ou’re“Yay orbidmay, Eorge,gay” aidsay ishay iendfray. is“Thay ashay eenbay aay ainstray otay
ouyay anday ouyay on’tday owknay atwhay ou’reyay ayingsay. Ou’dyay etterbay tryay anday itsay
uietqay illtay orning.may”

e“Hay urderedmay er.hay”

It“ay asway anay accidentay, Eorge.gay”

Ilsonway ookshay ishay eadhay. Ishay eyesay arrowednay anday ishay outhmay idenedway
ightlyslay ithway ethay ostghay ofay aay uperiorsay “Hm!ay”

I“ay ow,knay” ehay aidsay efinitelyday. I’m“ay oneay ofay esethay ustingtray ellasfay anday Iay
on’tday inkthay anyay armhay otay obodynay, utbay enwhay Iay etgay otay owknay aay ingthay Iay owknay
itay. Itay asway ethay anmay inay atthay arcay. Eshay anray outay otay eakspay otay imhay anday ehay
ouldn’tway op.stay”

Ichaelismay adhay eensay isthay ootay, utbay itay adn’thay occurreday otay imhay atthay erethay
asway anyay ecialspay ignificancesay inay itay. Ehay elievedbay atthay Mrsay. Ilsonway adhay
eenbay unningray awayay omfray erhay usbandhay, atherray anthay ingtryay otay opstay anyay
articularpay arcay.

ow“Hay ouldcay eshay ofay eenbay ikelay at?thay”

e’s“Shay aay eepday one,ay” aidsay Ilsonway, asay ifay atthay answereday ethay uestionqay.
Ah-h-h—“ay”

Ehay eganbay otay ockray againay, anday Ichaelismay oodstay istingtway ethay eashlay inay ishay
andhay.

aybe“May ouyay otgay omesay iendfray atthay Iay ouldcay elephonetay orfay, Eorge?gay”

Isthay asway aay orlornfay ope—hehay asway almostay uresay atthay Ilsonway adhay onay iendfray:
erethay asway otnay enoughay ofay imhay orfay ishay ifeway. Ehay asway adglay aay ittlelay aterlay
enwhay ehay oticednay aay angechay inay ethay oomray, aay ueblay uickeningqay byay ethay indowway,
anday ealizedray atthay awnday asn’tway arfay offay. Aboutay ivefay o’clockay itay asway ueblay
enoughay outsideay otay apsnay offay ethay ightlay.

Ilson’sway azedglay eyesay urnedtay outay otay ethay ash-heapsay, erewhay allsmay eygray
oudsclay ooktay onay antasticfay apesshay anday urriedscay erehay anday erethay inay ethay
aintfay awnday indway.

I“ay okespay otay er,hay” ehay utteredmay, afteray aay onglay ilencesay. I“ay oldtay erhay eshay
ightmay oolfay emay utbay eshay ouldn’tcay oolfay Odgay. Iay ooktay erhay otay ethay
indow”—withway anay effortay ehay otgay upay anday alkedway otay ethay earray indowway anday
eanedlay ithway ishay acefay essedpray againstay it—“anday Iay aidsay od‘Gay owsknay atwhay
ou’veyay eenbay oingday, everythingay ou’veyay eenbay oingday. Ouyay aymay oolfay emay, utbay
ouyay an’tcay oolfay Od!gay’ ”

Andingstay ehindbay imhay, Ichaelismay awsay ithway aay ockshay atthay ehay asway ookinglay atay
ethay eyesay ofay Octorday Tay. Jay. Eckleburgay, ichwhay adhay ustjay emergeday, alepay anday
enormousay, omfray ethay issolvingday ightnay.

od“Gay eessay everything,ay” epeatedray Ilsonway.

at’s“Thay anay advertisement,ay” Ichaelismay assureday imhay. Omethingsay ademay imhay
urntay awayay omfray ethay indowway anday ooklay ackbay intoay ethay oomray. Utbay Ilsonway
oodstay erethay aay onglay imetay, ishay acefay oseclay otay ethay indowway anepay, oddingnay
intoay ethay ilighttway.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Byay ixsay o’clockay Ichaelismay asway ornway outay, anday atefulgray orfay ethay oundsay ofay aay
arcay oppingstay outsideay. Itay asway oneay ofay ethay atchersway ofay ethay ightnay eforebay
owhay adhay omisedpray otay omecay ackbay, osay ehay ookedcay eakfastbray orfay eethray, ichwhay
ehay anday ethay otheray anmay ateay ogethertay. Ilsonway asway uieterqay ownay, anday
Ichaelismay entway omehay otay eepslay; enwhay ehay awokeay ourfay ourshay aterlay anday
urriedhay ackbay otay ethay aragegay, Ilsonway asway onegay.

Ishay ovements—hemay asway onay ootfay allay ethay ime—weretay afterwarday acedtray otay
Ortpay Ooseveltray anday enthay otay Ad’sgay Illhay, erewhay ehay oughtbay aay andwichsay atthay
ehay idn’tday eatay, anday aay upcay ofay offeecay. Ehay ustmay avehay eenbay iredtay anday
alkingway owlyslay, orfay ehay idn’tday eachray Ad’sgay Illhay untilay oonnay. Usthay arfay
erethay asway onay ifficultyday inay accountingay orfay ishay ime—theretay ereway oysbay owhay
adhay eensay aay anmay acting“ay ortsay ofay azy,cray” anday otoristsmay atay omwhay ehay aredstay
oddlyay omfray ethay idesay ofay ethay oadray. Enthay orfay eethray ourshay ehay isappearedday
omfray iewvay. Ethay olicepay, onay ethay engthstray ofay atwhay ehay aidsay otay Ichaelismay,
atthay ehay ad“hay aay ayway ofay indingfay out,ay” upposedsay atthay ehay entspay atthay imetay
oinggay omfray aragegay otay aragegay ereaboutthay, inquiringay orfay aay ellowyay arcay. Onay
ethay otheray andhay, onay aragegay anmay owhay adhay eensay imhay everay amecay orwardfay, anday
erhapspay ehay adhay anay easieray, urersay ayway ofay indingfay outay atwhay ehay antedway otay
owknay. Byay alf-pasthay otway ehay asway inay Estway Eggay, erewhay ehay askeday omeonesay ethay
ayway otay Atsby’sgay ousehay. Osay byay atthay imetay ehay ewknay Atsby’sgay amenay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Atay otway o’clockay Atsbygay utpay onay ishay athing-suitbay anday eftlay ordway ithway ethay
utlerbay atthay ifay anyoneay onedphay ordway asway otay ebay oughtbray otay imhay atay ethay
oolpay. Ehay oppedstay atay ethay aragegay orfay aay eumaticpnay attressmay atthay adhay
amuseday ishay uestsgay uringday ethay ummersay, anday ethay auffeurchay elpedhay imhay otay
umppay itay upay. Enthay ehay avegay instructionsay atthay ethay openay arcay asn’tway otay ebay
akentay outay underay anyay ircumstances—andcay isthay asway angestray, ecausebay ethay
ontfray ightray enderfay eedednay epairray.

Atsbygay oulderedshay ethay attressmay anday artedstay orfay ethay oolpay. Onceay ehay
oppedstay anday iftedshay itay aay ittlelay, anday ethay auffeurchay askeday imhay ifay ehay
eedednay elphay, utbay ehay ookshay ishay eadhay anday inay aay omentmay isappearedday amongay
ethay ellowingyay eestray.

Onay elephonetay essagemay arriveday, utbay ethay utlerbay entway ithoutway ishay eepslay
anday aitedway orfay itay untilay ourfay o’clock—untilay onglay afteray erethay asway anyoneay
otay ivegay itay otay ifay itay amecay. Iay avehay anay ideaay atthay Atsbygay imselfhay idn’tday
elievebay itay ouldway omecay, anday erhapspay ehay onay ongerlay aredcay. Ifay atthay asway
uetray ehay ustmay avehay eltfay atthay ehay adhay ostlay ethay olday armway orldway, aidpay aay
ighhay icepray orfay ivinglay ootay onglay ithway aay inglesay eamdray. Ehay ustmay avehay
ookedlay upay atay anay unfamiliaray skyay oughthray ighteningfray eaveslay anday iveredshay
asay ehay oundfay atwhay aay otesquegray ingthay aay oseray isay anday owhay awray ethay unlightsay
asway uponay ethay arcelyscay eatedcray assgray. Aay ewnay orldway, aterialmay ithoutway
eingbay ealray, erewhay oorpay ostsghay, eathingbray eamsdray ikelay airay, ifteddray
ortuitouslyfay aboutay … ikelay atthay ashenay, antasticfay igurefay idingglay owardtay
imhay oughthray ethay amorphousay eestray.

Ethay auffeur—hechay asway oneay ofay Olfshiem’sway otégés—heardpray ethay
ots—afterwardsshay ehay ouldcay onlyay aysay atthay ehay adn’thay oughtthay anythingay
uchmay aboutay emthay. Iay ovedray omfray ethay ationstay irectlyday otay Atsby’sgay ousehay
anday myay ushingray anxiouslyay upay ethay ontfray epsstay asway ethay irstfay ingthay atthay
alarmeday anyoneay. Utbay eythay ewknay enthay, Iay irmlyfay elievebay. Ithway arcelyscay aay
ordway aidsay, ourfay ofay usay, ethay auffeurchay, utlerbay, ardenergay, anday Iay urriedhay
ownday otay ethay oolpay.

Erethay asway aay aintfay, arelybay erceptiblepay ovementmay ofay ethay aterway asay ethay
eshfray owflay omfray oneay enday urgeday itsay ayway owardtay ethay aindray atay ethay otheray.
Ithway ittlelay ipplesray atthay ereway ardlyhay ethay adowsshay ofay avesway, ethay adenlay
attressmay ovedmay irregularlyay ownday ethay oolpay. Aay allsmay ustgay ofay indway atthay
arcelyscay orrugatedcay ethay urfacesay asway enoughay otay isturbday itsay accidentalay
oursecay ithway itsay accidentalay urdenbay. Ethay ouchtay ofay aay usterclay ofay eaveslay
evolvedray itay owlyslay, acingtray, ikelay ethay eglay ofay ansittray, aay inthay edray
irclecay inay ethay aterway.

Itay asway afteray eway artedstay ithway Atsbygay owardtay ethay ousehay atthay ethay ardenergay
awsay Ilson’sway odybay aay ittlelay ayway offay inay ethay assgray, anday ethay olocausthay asway
ompletecay.


IXay

Afteray otway earsyay Iay ememberray ethay estray ofay atthay ayday, anday atthay ightnay anday
ethay extnay ayday, onlyay asay anay endlessay illdray ofay olicepay anday otographersphay anday
ewspapernay enmay inay anday outay ofay Atsby’sgay ontfray oorday. Aay operay etchedstray
acrossay ethay ainmay ategay anday aay olicemanpay byay itay eptkay outay ethay uriouscay, utbay
ittlelay oysbay oonsay iscoveredday atthay eythay ouldcay enteray oughthray myay ardyay, anday
erethay ereway alwaysay aay ewfay ofay emthay usteredclay open-moutheday aboutay ethay
oolpay. Omeonesay ithway aay ositivepay annermay, erhapspay aay etectiveday, useday ethay
expressionay adman“may” asay ehay entbay overay Ilson’sway odybay atthay afternoonay, anday
ethay adventitiousay authorityay ofay ishay oicevay etsay ethay eykay orfay ethay ewspapernay
eportsray extnay orningmay.

Ostmay ofay osethay eportsray ereway aay ightmare—grotesquenay, ircumstantialcay,
eageray, anday untrueay. Enwhay Ichaelis’smay estimonytay atay ethay inquestay oughtbray
otay ightlay Ilson’sway uspicionssay ofay ishay ifeway Iay oughtthay ethay olewhay aletay
ouldway ortlyshay ebay ervedsay upay inay acyray asquinade—butpay Atherinecay, owhay ightmay
avehay aidsay anythingay, idn’tday aysay aay ordway. Eshay owedshay aay urprisingsay amountay
ofay aracterchay aboutay itay oo—lookedtay atay ethay oronercay ithway eterminedday eyesay
underay atthay orrectedcay owbray ofay ershay, anday oresway atthay erhay istersay adhay evernay
eensay Atsbygay, atthay erhay istersay asway ompletelycay appyhay ithway erhay usbandhay,
atthay erhay istersay adhay eenbay intoay onay ischiefmay ateverwhay. Eshay onvincedcay
erselfhay ofay itay, anday iedcray intoay erhay andkerchiefhay, asay ifay ethay eryvay
uggestionsay asway oremay anthay eshay ouldcay endureay. Osay Ilsonway asway educedray otay aay
anmay eranged“day byay iefgray” inay orderay atthay ethay asecay ightmay emainray inay itsay
implestsay ormfay. Anday itay estedray erethay.

Utbay allay isthay artpay ofay itay eemedsay emoteray anday unessentialay. Iay oundfay elfmysay
onay Atsby’sgay idesay, anday aloneay. Omfray ethay omentmay Iay elephonedtay ewsnay ofay ethay
atastrophecay otay Estway Eggay illagevay, everyay urmisesay aboutay imhay, anday everyay
acticalpray uestionqay, asway eferredray otay emay. Atay irstfay Iay asway urprisedsay anday
onfusedcay; enthay, asay ehay aylay inay ishay ousehay anday idn’tday ovemay oray eathebray oray
eakspay, ourhay uponay ourhay, itay ewgray uponay emay atthay Iay asway esponsibleray, ecausebay
onay oneay elseay asway interested—interesteday, Iay eanmay, ithway atthay intenseay
ersonalpay interestay otay ichwhay everyoneay ashay omesay aguevay ightray atay ethay enday.

Iay alledcay upay Aisyday alfhay anay ourhay afteray eway oundfay imhay, alledcay erhay
instinctivelyay anday ithoutway esitationhay. Utbay eshay anday Omtay adhay onegay awayay
earlyay atthay afternoonay, anday akentay aggagebay ithway emthay.

eft“Lay onay address?ay”

o.“Nay”

ay“Say enwhay ey’dthay ebay ack?bay”

o.“Nay”

Any“ay ideaay erewhay eythay areay? Owhay Iay ouldcay eachray em?thay”

I“ay on’tday owknay. An’tcay ay.say”

Iay antedway otay etgay omebodysay orfay imhay. Iay antedway otay ogay intoay ethay oomray erewhay
ehay aylay anday eassureray imhay: I’ll“ay etgay omebodysay orfay ouyay, Atsbygay. On’tday
orryway. Ustjay usttray emay anday I’llay etgay omebodysay orfay ou—yay”

Eyermay Olfshiem’sway amenay asn’tway inay ethay onephay ookbay. Ethay utlerbay avegay emay
ishay officeay addressay onay Oadwaybray, anday Iay alledcay Informationay, utbay byay ethay
imetay Iay adhay ethay umbernay itay asway onglay afteray ivefay, anday onay oneay answereday ethay
onephay.

ill“Way ouyay ingray again?ay”

I’ve“ay ungray eethray imes.tay”

It’s“ay eryvay important.ay”

orry“Say. I’may afraiday onay one’say ere.thay”

Iay entway ackbay otay ethay awing-roomdray anday oughtthay orfay anay instantay atthay eythay
ereway ancechay isitorsvay, allay esethay officialay eoplepay owhay uddenlysay illedfay
itay. Utbay, oughthay eythay ewdray ackbay ethay eetshay anday ookedlay atay Atsbygay ithway
ockedshay eyesay, ishay otestpray ontinuedcay inay myay ainbray:

ook“Lay erehay, olday ortspay, ou’veyay otgay otay etgay omebodysay orfay emay. Ou’veyay otgay
otay tryay ardhay. Iay an’tcay ogay oughthray isthay alone.ay”

Omeonesay artedstay otay askay emay uestionsqay, utbay Iay okebray awayay anday oinggay
upstairsay ookedlay astilyhay oughthray ethay unlockeday artspay ofay ishay esk—he’dday
evernay oldtay emay efinitelyday atthay ishay arentspay ereway eadday. Utbay erethay asway
othing—onlynay ethay icturepay ofay Anday Odycay, aay okentay ofay orgottenfay iolencevay,
aringstay ownday omfray ethay allway.

Extnay orningmay Iay entsay ethay utlerbay otay Ewnay Orkyay ithway aay etterlay otay Olfshiemway,
ichwhay askeday orfay informationay anday urgeday imhay otay omecay outay onay ethay extnay
aintray. Atthay equestray eemedsay uperfluoussay enwhay Iay otewray itay. Iay asway uresay
e’dhay artstay enwhay ehay awsay ethay ewspapersnay, ustjay asay Iay asway uresay ere’dthay ebay aay
ireway omfray Aisyday eforebay oon—butnay eithernay aay ireway ornay Mray. Olfshiemway
arriveday; onay oneay arriveday exceptay oremay olicepay anday otographersphay anday
ewspapernay enmay. Enwhay ethay utlerbay oughtbray ackbay Olfshiem’sway answeray Iay eganbay
otay avehay aay eelingfay ofay efianceday, ofay ornfulscay olidaritysay etweenbay Atsbygay
anday emay againstay emthay allay.

Earday Mray. Arrawaycay. Isthay ashay eenbay oneay ofay ethay ostmay erribletay ocksshay ofay
myay ifelay otay emay Iay ardlyhay ancay elievebay itay atthay itay isay uetray atay allay. Uchsay aay
admay actay asay atthay anmay idday ouldshay akemay usay allay inkthay. Iay annotcay omecay ownday
ownay asay Iay amay iedtay upay inay omesay eryvay importantay usinessbay anday annotcay etgay
ixedmay upay inay isthay ingthay ownay. Ifay erethay isay anythingay Iay ancay oday aay ittlelay
aterlay etlay emay owknay inay aay etterlay byay Edgaray. Iay ardlyhay owknay erewhay Iay amay enwhay
Iay earhay aboutay aay ingthay ikelay isthay anday amay ompletelycay ockedknay ownday anday
outay.

Oursyay ulytray

Eyermay Olfshiemway

anday enthay astyhay addendaay eneathbay:

Etlay emay owknay aboutay ethay uneralfay etcay oday otnay owknay ishay amilyfay atay allay.

Enwhay ethay onephay angray atthay afternoonay anday Onglay Istanceday aidsay Icagochay asway
allingcay Iay oughtthay isthay ouldway ebay Aisyday atay astlay. Utbay ethay onnectioncay amecay
oughthray asay aay an’smay oicevay, eryvay inthay anday arfay awayay.

is“Thay isay Agleslay eakingspay …ay”

es?“Yay” Ethay amenay asway unfamiliaray.

ell“Hay ofay aay otenay, isn’tay itay? Etgay myay ire?way”

ere“Thay aven’thay eenbay anyay ires.way”

oung“Yay Arke’spay inay ouble,tray” ehay aidsay apidlyray. ey“Thay ickedpay imhay upay enwhay
ehay andedhay ethay ondsbay overay ethay ountercay. Eythay otgay aay ircularcay omfray Ewnay
Orkyay ivinggay em’ay ethay umbersnay ustjay ivefay inutesmay eforebay. Atwhay oud’yay owknay
aboutay atthay, eyhay? Ouyay evernay ancay elltay inay esethay ickhay owns—tay”

ello!“Hay” Iay interrupteday eathlesslybray. ook“Lay ere—thishay isn’tay Mray.
Atsbygay. Mray. Atsby’sgay ead.day”

Erethay asway aay onglay ilencesay onay ethay otheray enday ofay ethay ireway, ollowedfay byay anay
exclamationay … enthay aay uickqay uawksqay asay ethay onnectioncay asway okenbray.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Iay inkthay itay asway onay ethay irdthay ayday atthay aay elegramtay ignedsay Enryhay Cay. Atzgay
arriveday omfray aay owntay inay Innesotamay. Itay aidsay onlyay atthay ethay endersay asway
eavinglay immediatelyay anday otay ostponepay ethay uneralfay untilay ehay amecay.

Itay asway Atsby’sgay atherfay, aay olemnsay olday anmay, eryvay elplesshay anday ismayedday,
undledbay upay inay aay onglay eapchay ulsteray againstay ethay armway Eptembersay ayday. Ishay
eyesay eakedlay ontinuouslycay ithway excitementay, anday enwhay Iay ooktay ethay agbay anday
umbrellaay omfray ishay andshay ehay eganbay otay ullpay osay incessantlyay atay ishay arsespay
eygray eardbay atthay Iay adhay ifficultyday inay ettinggay offay ishay oatcay. Ehay asway onay
ethay ointpay ofay ollapsecay, osay Iay ooktay imhay intoay ethay usic-roommay anday ademay imhay
itsay ownday ilewhay Iay entsay orfay omethingsay otay eatay. Utbay ehay ouldn’tway eatay, anday
ethay assglay ofay ilkmay illedspay omfray ishay emblingtray andhay.

I“ay awsay itay inay ethay Icagochay ewspaper,nay” ehay aidsay. It“ay asway allay inay ethay
Icagochay ewspapernay. Iay artedstay ightray away.ay”

I“ay idn’tday owknay owhay otay eachray ou.yay”

Ishay eyesay, eeingsay othingnay, ovedmay easelesslycay aboutay ethay oomray.

It“ay asway aay adman,may” ehay aidsay. e“Hay ustmay avehay eenbay ad.may”

ouldn’t“Way ouyay ikelay omesay offee?cay” Iay urgeday imhay.

I“ay on’tday antway anythingay. I’may allay ightray ownay, Mr.—ay”

arraway.“Cay”

ell“Way, I’may allay ightray ownay. Erewhay avehay eythay otgay Immy?jay”

Iay ooktay imhay intoay ethay awing-roomdray, erewhay ishay onsay aylay, anday eftlay imhay
erethay. Omesay ittlelay oysbay adhay omecay upay onay ethay epsstay anday ereway ookinglay intoay
ethay allhay; enwhay Iay oldtay emthay owhay adhay arriveday, eythay entway eluctantlyray
awayay.

Afteray aay ittlelay ilewhay Mray. Atzgay openeday ethay oorday anday amecay outay, ishay outhmay
ajaray, ishay acefay ushedflay ightlyslay, ishay eyesay eakinglay isolateday anday
unpunctualay earstay. Ehay adhay eachedray anay ageay erewhay eathday onay ongerlay ashay ethay
ualityqay ofay astlyghay urprisesay, anday enwhay ehay ookedlay arounday imhay ownay orfay ethay
irstfay imetay anday awsay ethay eighthay anday endoursplay ofay ethay allhay anday ethay eatgray
oomsray openingay outay omfray itay intoay otheray oomsray, ishay iefgray eganbay otay ebay
ixedmay ithway anay aweday idepray. Iay elpedhay imhay otay aay edroombay upstairsay; ilewhay ehay
ooktay offay ishay oatcay anday estvay Iay oldtay imhay atthay allay arrangementsay adhay eenbay
eferredday untilay ehay amecay.
