Oneay ofay myay ostmay ividvay emoriesmay isay ofay omingcay ackbay Estway omfray eppray oolschay
anday aterlay omfray ollegecay atay Istmaschray imetay. Osethay owhay entway artherfay anthay
Icagochay ouldway athergay inay ethay olday imday Unionay Ationstay atay ixsay o’clockay ofay aay
Ecemberday eveningay, ithway aay ewfay Icagochay iendsfray, alreadyay aughtcay upay intoay
eirthay ownay olidayhay aietiesgay, otay idbay emthay aay astyhay oodbyegay. Iay ememberray
ethay urfay oatscay ofay ethay irlsgay eturningray omfray Issmay Is-or-That’sthay anday ethay
atterchay ofay ozenfray eathbray anday ethay andshay avingway overheaday asay eway aughtcay
ightsay ofay olday acquaintancesay, anday ethay atchingsmay ofay invitationsay: Are“ay ouyay
oinggay otay ethay Ordways’ay? ethay Erseys’hay? ethay Ultzes’?schay” anday ethay onglay
eengray icketstay aspedclay ighttay inay ouray ovedglay andshay. Anday astlay ethay urkymay
ellowyay arscay ofay ethay Icagochay, Ilwaukeemay anday Stay. Aulpay ailroadray ookinglay
eerfulchay asay Istmaschray itselfay onay ethay ackstray esidebay ethay ategay.

Enwhay eway ulledpay outay intoay ethay interway ightnay anday ethay ealray owsnay, ouray owsnay,
eganbay otay etchstray outay esidebay usay anday inkletway againstay ethay indowsway, anday
ethay imday ightslay ofay allsmay Isconsinway ationsstay ovedmay byay, aay arpshay ildway
acebray amecay uddenlysay intoay ethay airay. Eway ewdray inay eepday eathsbray ofay itay asay eway
alkedway ackbay omfray innerday oughthray ethay oldcay estibulesvay, unutterablyay awareay
ofay ouray identityay ithway isthay ountrycay orfay oneay angestray ourhay, eforebay eway
eltedmay indistinguishablyay intoay itay againay.

At’sthay myay Iddlemay Est—notway ethay eatwhay oray ethay airiespray oray ethay ostlay Edesway
ownstay, utbay ethay illingthray eturningray ainstray ofay myay outhyay, anday ethay eetstray
ampslay anday eighslay ellsbay inay ethay ostyfray arkday anday ethay adowsshay ofay ollyhay
eathswray ownthray byay ightedlay indowsway onay ethay owsnay. Iay amay artpay ofay atthay, aay
ittlelay olemnsay ithway ethay eelfay ofay osethay onglay intersway, aay ittlelay omplacentcay
omfray owinggray upay inay ethay Arrawaycay ousehay inay aay itycay erewhay ellingsdway areay
illstay alledcay oughthray ecadesday byay aay amily’sfay amenay. Iay eesay ownay atthay isthay
ashay eenbay aay orystay ofay ethay Estway, afteray all—Tomay anday Atsbygay, Aisyday anday
Ordanjay anday Iay, ereway allay Esternersway, anday erhapspay eway ossessedpay omesay
eficiencyday inay ommoncay ichwhay ademay usay ubtlysay unadaptableay otay Easternay ifelay.

Evenay enwhay ethay Eastay exciteday emay ostmay, evenay enwhay Iay asway ostmay eenlykay awareay
ofay itsay uperioritysay otay ethay oredbay, awlingspray, ollensway ownstay eyondbay ethay
Ohioay, ithway eirthay interminableay inquisitionsay ichwhay aredspay onlyay ethay
ildrenchay anday ethay eryvay old—evenay enthay itay adhay alwaysay orfay emay aay ualityqay ofay
istortionday. Estway Eggay, especiallyay, illstay iguresfay inay myay oremay antasticfay
eamsdray. Iay eesay itay asay aay ightnay enescay byay Elay Ecogray: aay undredhay ouseshay, atay
onceay onventionalcay anday otesquegray, ouchingcray underay aay ullensay, overhangingay
skyay anday aay ustrelesslay oonmay. Inay ethay oregroundfay ourfay olemnsay enmay inay essdray
uitssay areay alkingway alongay ethay idewalksay ithway aay etcherstray onay ichwhay ieslay aay
unkendray omanway inay aay itewhay eveningay essdray. Erhay andhay, ichwhay anglesday overay
ethay idesay, arklesspay oldcay ithway ewelsjay. Avelygray ethay enmay urntay inay atay aay
ouse—thehay ongwray ousehay. Utbay onay oneay owsknay ethay oman’sway amenay, anday onay oneay
arescay.

Afteray Atsby’sgay eathday ethay Eastay asway auntedhay orfay emay ikelay atthay, istortedday
eyondbay myay eyesay’ owerpay ofay orrectioncay. Osay enwhay ethay ueblay okesmay ofay ittlebray
eaveslay asway inay ethay airay anday ethay indway ewblay ethay etway aundrylay iffstay onay ethay
inelay Iay ecidedday otay omecay ackbay omehay.

Erethay asway oneay ingthay otay ebay oneday eforebay Iay eftlay, anay awkwarday, unpleasantay
ingthay atthay erhapspay adhay etterbay avehay eenbay etlay aloneay. Utbay Iay antedway otay
eavelay ingsthay inay orderay anday otnay ustjay usttray atthay obligingay anday indifferentay
easay otay eepsway myay efuseray awayay. Iay awsay Ordanjay Akerbay anday alkedtay overay anday
arounday atwhay adhay appenedhay otay usay ogethertay, anday atwhay adhay appenedhay
afterwarday otay emay, anday eshay aylay erfectlypay illstay, isteninglay, inay aay igbay
airchay.

Eshay asway esseddray otay ayplay olfgay, anday Iay ememberray inkingthay eshay ookedlay ikelay
aay oodgay illustrationay, erhay inchay aisedray aay ittlelay auntilyjay, erhay airhay ethay
olourcay ofay anay autumnay eaflay, erhay acefay ethay amesay ownbray inttay asay ethay
ingerlessfay oveglay onay erhay eeknay. Enwhay Iay adhay inishedfay eshay oldtay emay ithoutway
ommentcay atthay eshay asway engageday otay anotheray anmay. Iay oubtedday atthay, oughthay
erethay ereway everalsay eshay ouldcay avehay arriedmay atay aay odnay ofay erhay eadhay, utbay Iay
etendedpray otay ebay urprisedsay. Orfay ustjay aay inutemay Iay onderedway ifay Iay asn’tway
akingmay aay istakemay, enthay Iay oughtthay itay allay overay againay uicklyqay anday otgay upay
otay aysay oodbyegay.

evertheless“Nay ouyay idday owthray emay over,ay” aidsay Ordanjay uddenlysay. ou“Yay ewthray
emay overay onay ethay elephonetay. Iay on’tday ivegay aay amnday aboutay ouyay ownay, utbay itay
asway aay ewnay experienceay orfay emay, anday Iay eltfay aay ittlelay izzyday orfay aay ile.whay”

Eway ookshay andshay.

Oh“ay, anday oday ouyay emember”—sheray added—“aay onversationcay eway adhay onceay aboutay
ivingdray aay ar?cay”

ot“Why—nay exactly.ay”

ou“Yay aidsay aay adbay iverdray asway onlyay afesay untilay eshay etmay anotheray adbay iverdray?
Ellway, Iay etmay anotheray adbay iverdray, idn’tday Iay? Iay eanmay itay asway arelesscay ofay emay
otay akemay uchsay aay ongwray uessgay. Iay oughtthay ouyay ereway atherray anay onesthay,
aightforwardstray ersonpay. Iay oughtthay itay asway ouryay ecretsay ide.pray”

I’m“ay irty,thay” Iay aidsay. I’m“ay ivefay earsyay ootay olday otay ielay otay elfmysay anday
allcay itay onour.hay”

Eshay idn’tday answeray. Angryay, anday alfhay inay ovelay ithway erhay, anday emendouslytray
orrysay, Iay urnedtay awayay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Oneay afternoonay atelay inay Octoberay Iay awsay Omtay Uchananbay. Ehay asway alkingway aheaday
ofay emay alongay Ifthfay Avenueay inay ishay alertay, aggressiveay ayway, ishay andshay outay aay
ittlelay omfray ishay odybay asay ifay otay ightfay offay interferenceay, ishay eadhay ovingmay
arplyshay erehay anday erethay, adaptingay itselfay otay ishay estlessray eyesay. Ustjay asay
Iay owedslay upay otay avoiday overtakingay imhay ehay oppedstay anday eganbay owningfray intoay
ethay indowsway ofay aay ewelleryjay orestay. Uddenlysay ehay awsay emay anday alkedway ackbay,
oldinghay outay ishay andhay.

at’s“Whay ethay attermay, Icknay? Oday ouyay objectay otay akingshay andshay ithway e?may”

es“Yay. Ouyay owknay atwhay Iay inkthay ofay ou.yay”

ou’re“Yay azycray, Ick,nay” ehay aidsay uicklyqay. azy“Cray asay ellhay. Iay on’tday owknay
at’swhay ethay attermay ithway ou.yay”

om,“Tay” Iay inquireday, at“whay idday ouyay aysay otay Ilsonway atthay afternoon?ay”

Ehay aredstay atay emay ithoutway aay ordway, anday Iay ewknay Iay adhay uessedgay ightray aboutay
osethay issingmay ourshay. Iay artedstay otay urntay awayay, utbay ehay ooktay aay epstay afteray
emay anday abbedgray myay armay.

I“ay oldtay imhay ethay uth,tray” ehay aidsay. e“Hay amecay otay ethay oorday ilewhay eway ereway
ettinggay eadyray otay eavelay, anday enwhay Iay entsay ownday ordway atthay eway eren’tway inay
ehay iedtray otay orcefay ishay ayway upstairsay. Ehay asway azycray enoughay otay illkay emay ifay
Iay adn’thay oldtay imhay owhay owneday ethay arcay. Ishay andhay asway onay aay evolverray inay ishay
ocketpay everyay inutemay ehay asway inay ethay ouse—hay” Ehay okebray offay efiantlyday.
at“Whay ifay Iay idday elltay imhay? Atthay ellowfay adhay itay omingcay otay imhay. Ehay ewthray
ustday intoay ouryay eyesay ustjay ikelay ehay idday inay Aisy’sday, utbay ehay asway aay oughtay
oneay. Ehay anray overay Emyrtlay ikelay ou’dyay unray overay aay ogday anday evernay evenay
oppedstay ishay ar.cay”

Erethay asway othingnay Iay ouldcay aysay, exceptay ethay oneay unutterableay actfay atthay itay
asn’tway uetray.

And“ay ifay ouyay inkthay Iay idn’tday avehay myay areshay ofay uffering—looksay erehay, enwhay
Iay entway otay ivegay upay atthay atflay anday awsay atthay amnday oxbay ofay ogday iscuitsbay
ittingsay erethay onay ethay ideboardsay, Iay atsay ownday anday iedcray ikelay aay abybay. Byay
Odgay itay asway awful—ay”

Iay ouldn’tcay orgivefay imhay oray ikelay imhay, utbay Iay awsay atthay atwhay ehay adhay oneday
asway, otay imhay, entirelyay ustifiedjay. Itay asway allay eryvay arelesscay anday
onfusedcay. Eythay ereway arelesscay eoplepay, Omtay anday Aisy—theyday ashedsmay upay
ingsthay anday eaturescray anday enthay etreatedray ackbay intoay eirthay oneymay oray eirthay
astvay arelessnesscay, oray ateverwhay itay asway atthay eptkay emthay ogethertay, anday etlay
otheray eoplepay eanclay upay ethay essmay eythay adhay ademay …

Iay ookshay andshay ithway imhay; itay eemedsay illysay otnay otay, orfay Iay eltfay uddenlysay asay
oughthay Iay ereway alkingtay otay aay ildchay. Enthay ehay entway intoay ethay ewelleryjay
orestay otay uybay aay earlpay ecklace—ornay erhapspay onlyay aay airpay ofay uffcay
uttons—ridbay ofay myay ovincialpray ueamishnesssqay oreverfay.

-----------------------------------------------------------------------ay-

Atsby’sgay ousehay asway illstay emptyay enwhay Iay eft—thelay assgray onay ishay awnlay adhay
owngray asay onglay asay inemay. Oneay ofay ethay axitay iversdray inay ethay illagevay evernay
ooktay aay arefay astpay ethay entranceay ategay ithoutway oppingstay orfay aay inutemay anday
ointingpay insideay; erhapspay itay asway ehay owhay ovedray Aisyday anday Atsbygay overay otay
Eastay Eggay ethay ightnay ofay ethay accidentay, anday erhapspay ehay adhay ademay aay orystay
aboutay itay allay ishay ownay. Iay idn’tday antway otay earhay itay anday Iay avoideday imhay enwhay
Iay otgay offay ethay aintray.

Iay entspay myay Aturdaysay ightsnay inay Ewnay Orkyay ecausebay osethay eamingglay,
azzlingday artiespay ofay ishay ereway ithway emay osay ividlyvay atthay Iay ouldcay illstay
earhay ethay usicmay anday ethay aughterlay, aintfay anday incessantay, omfray ishay ardengay,
anday ethay arscay oinggay upay anday ownday ishay ivedray. Oneay ightnay Iay idday earhay aay
aterialmay arcay erethay, anday awsay itsay ightslay opstay atay ishay ontfray epsstay. Utbay Iay
idn’tday investigateay. Obablypray itay asway omesay inalfay uestgay owhay adhay eenbay awayay
atay ethay endsay ofay ethay earthay anday idn’tday owknay atthay ethay artypay asway overay.

Onay ethay astlay ightnay, ithway myay unktray ackedpay anday myay arcay oldsay otay ethay ocergray,
Iay entway overay anday ookedlay atay atthay ugehay incoherentay ailurefay ofay aay ousehay onceay
oremay. Onay ethay itewhay epsstay anay obsceneay ordway, awledscray byay omesay oybay ithway aay
iecepay ofay ickbray, oodstay outay earlyclay inay ethay oonlightmay, anday Iay eraseday itay,
awingdray myay oeshay aspinglyray alongay ethay onestay. Enthay Iay anderedway ownday otay ethay
eachbay anday awledspray outay onay ethay andsay.

Ostmay ofay ethay igbay oreshay acesplay ereway osedclay ownay anday erethay ereway ardlyhay anyay
ightslay exceptay ethay adowyshay, ovingmay owglay ofay aay erryboatfay acrossay ethay
Oundsay. Anday asay ethay oonmay oseray igherhay ethay inessentialay ouseshay eganbay otay
eltmay awayay untilay aduallygray Iay ecamebay awareay ofay ethay olday islanday erehay atthay
oweredflay onceay orfay Utchday ailorssay’ eyes—aay eshfray, eengray eastbray ofay ethay ewnay
orldway. Itsay anishedvay eestray, ethay eestray atthay adhay ademay ayway orfay Atsby’sgay
ousehay, adhay onceay anderedpay inay isperswhay otay ethay astlay anday eatestgray ofay allay
umanhay eamsdray; orfay aay ansitorytray enchanteday omentmay anmay ustmay avehay eldhay ishay
eathbray inay ethay esencepray ofay isthay ontinentcay, ompelledcay intoay anay aestheticay
ontemplationcay ehay eithernay understooday ornay esiredday, acefay otay acefay orfay ethay
astlay imetay inay istoryhay ithway omethingsay ommensuratecay otay ishay apacitycay orfay
onderway.

Anday asay Iay atsay erethay oodingbray onay ethay olday, unknownay orldway, Iay oughtthay ofay
Atsby’sgay onderway enwhay ehay irstfay ickedpay outay ethay eengray ightlay atay ethay enday ofay
Aisy’sday ockday. Ehay adhay omecay aay onglay ayway otay isthay ueblay awnlay, anday ishay eamdray
ustmay avehay eemedsay osay oseclay atthay ehay ouldcay ardlyhay ailfay otay aspgray itay. Ehay
idday otnay owknay atthay itay asway alreadyay ehindbay imhay, omewheresay ackbay inay atthay
astvay obscurityay eyondbay ethay itycay, erewhay ethay arkday ieldsfay ofay ethay epublicray
olledray onay underay ethay ightnay.

Atsbygay elievedbay inay ethay eengray ightlay, ethay orgiasticay uturefay atthay earyay byay
earyay ecedesray eforebay usay. Itay eludeday usay enthay, utbay at’sthay onay

oneay inefay orningmay—
